The Stage-One workup's note that her ceiling is grief, not fury, remains the operating assumption.

## 10. Current State — Summary

Muneeba Khan, present day: a woman in her early-to-mid fifties, observant, married, mother of two living adult children (both now disclosed as superhuman, one mutant-disclosed posthumously and resurrected, the other late-emerging), grandmother of one, anchor of a Jersey City household that has absorbed catastrophe and reconstituted around it. Health: normative. Affect: contained at baseline, warmer in the domestic register than at any prior canonical period, openly tender with the grandchild. Practice: deepened. Marriage: closer. Parenting: looser on the surface, denser underneath. Community: intact and supportive. The container, tested by the worst event her file contemplates, held; and the woman who emerged from the test has not become harder but, by the granular evidence, slightly and consistently softer.

She is, at present file-date, the most fully integrated version of herself the published record has yet shown. Whether that integration is stable or transitional is the question the next chronology will have to answer.

*End Chronology IV. Continue to thematic synthesis.*


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — MUNEEBA KHAN

*UATU Dossier, Section 2 of N. Source basis: G. Willow Wilson run on* Ms. Marvel *(2014–2019); Saladin Ahmed's* Magnificent Ms. Marvel *(2019–2021); the bereavement arcs of 2022–2023 (*The Death of Ms. Marvel*, *Fallen Friend*); and the post-resurrection material (*Ms. Marvel: The New Mutant*). Where the canonical record is silent, the file flags inference explicitly and reasons from cohort epidemiology and depicted somatic behavior. This section is exhaustive on purpose: a total-surveillance file does not omit the body.*

---

## 2.1 OVERVIEW AND BASELINE PHENOTYPE

Subject is a Pakistani-American woman, first depicted in her mid-to-late forties (2014) and aging in approximate publication-time through her early-to-mid fifties by the post-resurrection material. Born in Karachi (inferred from Yusuf's references and the family's emigration narrative); arrival in the United States as a young married woman in the late 1980s or early 1990s; resident of Jersey City, New Jersey, throughout the published record.

**Anthropometric and constitutional:** average stature, full-figured by the artistic register Alphona, Miyazawa, Leon, and Jung successively establish; weight stable across the entire run with no depicted gain or loss of clinical significance. Skin South Asian Fitzpatrick IV; hair black, going to a few visible silver strands at the temples by the Ahmed run, almost always under hijab in public and visible only in domestic kitchen-table scenes. No glasses in early canon; reading glasses appear by mid-Ahmed run when she is depicted at the kitchen table with bills or the Qur'an, a quiet inference of presbyopia in the expected decade.

**Dominance:** right-handed (depicted stirring, writing, gesturing).

**Voice:** soft mezzo, code-switching between unaccented English with her children and Urdu with Yusuf and the auntie circle; no depicted dysphonia, no smoker's rasp.

**Resting somatic signature:** still hands when listening, busy hands when thinking. Stress shows in the **hands first** — wiping them on a dish towel that does not need wiping, smoothing her dupatta, rearranging cutlery on a set table. This is the most consistent somatic tell in the file across five years of writers and seven pencillers.

---

## 2.2 ABSENT OR ASSUMED-NEGATIVE CONDITIONS

The dossier is unusual among Jersey City Khan-family files in that the **negative findings are themselves diagnostic of a self-care pattern**. The published record contains:

- **No diabetes mellitus**, despite the elevated South Asian Type II prevalence and a household kitchen depicted as carbohydrate-rich (parathas, biryani, gulab jamun for milestone scenes). Inference: either undisclosed subclinical pre-diabetes managed silently (consistent with her containment habit; see §2.7), or genuinely intact metabolic health. The latter is plausible given depicted activity — she is rarely seated, almost always cooking, cleaning, ferrying, hosting.
- **No hypertension** explicitly named, though her depicted vigilance over **Yusuf's** blood pressure (cuff and pill bottles visible in the Ahmed run's domestic backgrounds) suggests household familiarity with the monitoring routine.
- **No thyroid disorder, no autoimmune condition, no chronic pain syndrome.**
- **No depicted dental issue, no surgical scarring, no orthopedic impairment.** Her gait is steady across all depictions.
- **No substance use of any kind.** No alcohol (consistent with observant practice), no tobacco, no recreational cannabis, no prescribed benzodiazepines or hypnotics even during the bereavement arc when a less devout cohort-matched mother would plausibly have been offered them. **The absence of pharmaceutical anxiolysis during the burial of a child is the single most clinically loud datum in the medical file.** It is not stoicism for performance; it is the structural refusal to outsource affect-regulation to a substance. (See §2.7.)
- **No caffeine excess.** Tea (chai) is depicted ritually rather than instrumentally — a vehicle for sitting with someone, not a stimulant managed for output.

The pattern: a body kept *unmedicalized* by deliberate routine. This is itself the medical history.

---

## 2.3 REPRODUCTIVE AND OBSTETRIC HISTORY

Two living births: **Aamir** (elder, by approximately five to seven years) and **Kamala** (younger, born in Jersey City circa 2000). No depicted miscarriage, no fertility intervention, no postpartum complication referenced in dialogue. The five-to-seven year inter-birth interval is wider than the South Asian first-generation modal pattern and is consistent either with deliberate spacing or with an undisclosed intervening loss; the canonical record does not adjudicate, but the **slight, recurrent tenderness Muneeba shows around Aamir's milestones — visibly disproportionate to the milestone itself** — is the kind of micro-signature a complete file would flag for possible unresolved interval grief. Inference, not finding.

Menstrual and menopausal status: unaddressed in canon. By the Ahmed run she is at or past the median age of menopause for her cohort; no symptom-cluster (hot flashes, sleep disturbance, mood lability) is ever depicted, which is either a writer-level omission or a behavior-consistent suppression on her part.

Breastfeeding history inferred from cultural pattern; no canonical confirmation.

No depicted gynecologic surgery. No hysterectomy. No mammographic anxiety on-page, though her age cohort puts her firmly in screening territory.

**Sexual health:** the marriage to Yusuf is depicted as warm, partnered, and physically affectionate within the modesty register canon uses for the household — hand-holding, foreheads-together, the small of the back. No dysfunction implied, no estrangement, no infidelity in either direction.

---

## 2.4 INFECTIOUS DISEASE, IMMUNIZATION, AND TRAVEL

Childhood immunization presumed complete per Pakistani schedule of the 1960s–70s (BCG scar inferable but never depicted on-panel). Adult exposures inferable from travel: at least one return to Karachi in the published era (referenced as family obligation), with attendant exposure baseline (enteric pathogens, dengue endemicity) but no depicted illness following. No COVID-era arc engages her specifically; the household is depicted as observant of community precaution during the relevant publication window.

No depicted hospitalization for infection.

---

## 2.5 INJURIES AND ACUTE EVENTS

The canonical record contains **no depicted injury to Muneeba's person**. She is not assaulted, not collateral-damaged by the considerable supervillain traffic her daughter draws to Jersey City, not hospitalized. This is statistically improbable given that she lives in a household with a costumed superhero and is at the geographic epicenter of multiple incursions, and it is best read as authorial protection of her function as the household's stable referent.

**Inferable minor record** (the kind of granular detail a full surveillance file would carry): the recurrent burns and small cuts of a daily cook. Her left thumb is depicted, in at least two domestic kitchen panels across the run, with a bandage that no scene ever explains. The micro-injury portrait of a woman who handles hot oil, knives, and the rim of a pressure cooker daily for thirty-plus years is the implicit background. No tendinopathy, no carpal tunnel signs depicted, despite the use pattern that predicts them.

**Acute psychological-physiological events:**

- **The Incursion (*Last Days*, 2015):** subject experiences what she believes to be the end of the world. Somatic presentation on-page: composed exterior, **physical reaching for her daughter** — the contact-seeking is the data. No depicted panic, no hyperventilation, no syncope. She *prays*. This becomes the template.
- **Yusuf's cardiac event (Ahmed run):** subject is the first responder in household terms. Her on-panel behavior is procedural — phone, ambulance, coat, keys — with affect visibly suppressed until the immediate crisis is past, at which point she is depicted briefly alone with her hands flat on a counter. This is the **counter-bracing posture** and recurs at every subsequent crisis point in the file. It is her single most reliable somatic tell of overwhelm.
- **Kamala's death:** see §2.7.

---

## 2.6 YUSUF'S CARDIAC ILLNESS AS PROXY MEDICAL HISTORY

Although clinically Yusuf's file, the cardiac event functionally appears in Muneeba's record because she absorbs the totality of its logistical and emotional load. Post-event, she is depicted: managing his medication schedule (a pill organizer appears in the kitchen background and persists across subsequent issues — a continuity detail that several artists preserved); modifying the household cooking (less ghee, more depicted vegetable preparation, though the change is small and never lectured at); and instituting a quiet veto over stressors that reach him — most pointedly, **filtering what Kamala-related crises he is told about and when**.

The medical-psychological consequence for Muneeba: a permanent recalibration of her threat model. Prior to the cardiac event, mortality was a religious abstraction; after it, it is a household variable she manages. The shift is visible in the increased frequency of her **morning du'a depicted at the kitchen window** — a behavior present occasionally in the Wilson run, near-daily by the late Ahmed run.

**No depicted caregiver burnout symptom cluster.** Again, the absence is the finding.

---

## 2.7 BEREAVEMENT: THE MEDICAL FILE OF KAMALA'S DEATH

The single most consequential entry in the medical history. The dossier treats it as a clinical event because it is one.

**Acute phase (first week):** subject depicted as physically present, verbally minimal. Eating is not shown; the absence is conspicuous in a household whose every emotional beat for a decade has been mediated by food. Sleep is not depicted. The counter-bracing posture from the Yusuf event recurs, repeatedly. She does not collapse. She does not scream. She receives mourners — the masjid circle, the aunties, neighbors — and she performs the ghusl-and-shrouding role with the women of the community (inferable from cultural pattern; the published record honors the privacy of the act).

**Sub-acute phase (first months):** the published record shows controlled public presentation and devastating private moments — a panel of her alone in Kamala's room, hands flat on the bed (counter-bracing again, transposed); a panel of her at the kitchen window at dawn. No depicted weeping in crowd. No depicted breakdown. The grief is metabolized through religious practice (du'a, Qur'an recitation, the structured rhythm of prayer times) and through **resumed cooking** — the moment she returns to the stove is, in the visual grammar of the book, her re-entry into functional life.

**Chronic phase and the mutant/resurrection arc:** subject does not develop the classic complicated-grief profile (yearning, identity disruption, avoidance of reminders, role-collapse). She integrates. The resurrection itself produces, in the *New Mutant* material, a response that is **not euphoria but a quieter, more guarded acceptance** — consistent with a woman who has already done the work of burying her child once and will not let her body be torn open a second time by hope. This guardedness is medically significant: it is the somatic signature of a grief that was *processed*, not bypassed.

**No depicted use of pharmaceuticals, no depicted alcohol breach, no depicted somatization (no new headaches, no GI complaints, no insomnia escalation visible on-page), no depicted weight change, no depicted withdrawal from prayer or community.** The container held. The dossier's earlier read — that her control is a chosen operational mode rather than a brittle defense — is most strongly substantiated here. A brittle container does not survive the death of a youngest child without symptomatic leakage. Hers did.

**Caveat the file is obligated to flag:** the published record is finite. A complete surveillance file would expect — and look for — delayed somatic emergence in the 18-to-36-month post-loss window, particularly cardiac (the broken-heart phenomenon, takotsubo, is over-represented in bereaved older women), endocrine (cortisol-driven metabolic shifts), and immune (latent viral reactivation). None is depicted. The dossier records this as **unobserved, not absent**.

---

## 2.8 TRANSFORMATIONS, ENHANCEMENT, EXPOSURE

Subject has **no powers, no augmentation, no Terrigen exposure, no mutant expression, no cosmic contact, no symbiote, no magical contract, no cybernetic implant.** She is, in a household and a city saturated with extraordinary biology, **deliberately and consistently ordinary**. This is itself a medical fact about her: she is the household's biological control variable, the unmodified reference point against which Kamala's polymorph physiology, Aamir's later Inhuman exposure questions, and the family's Krakoa-era entanglements are measured.

No depicted exposure to the Terrigen Mist cloud that activated Kamala, despite geographic proximity. The narrative explanation is latent-gene absence; the dossier records the non-event.

No transformation. No enhancement. No exposure. The body is the body.

---

## 2.9 SENSORY, COGNITIVE, AND NEUROLOGICAL

No depicted hearing loss, no visual impairment beyond the inferred presbyopia (§2.1). No depicted migraine. No depicted seizure. No depicted cognitive decline, no word-finding difficulty, no episodic disorientation. Memory across the run is **functionally photographic for household and community detail** — she tracks who said what at which gathering, what Auntie Ruby's daughter wore to which wedding, which of Kamala's friends has which allergy. This is not depicted as effortful; it is depicted as baseline.

No depicted sleep disorder. Her dawn-window scenes suggest **early waking consistent with Fajr observance**, which the file declines to pathologize — it is a chosen schedule, not insomnia.

---

## 2.10 INTEGRATIVE READ

The medical history of Muneeba Khan is, against the gravitational pull of her circumstances, **the medical history of a woman who has refused to become a patient**. She has buried a child, nursed a husband through cardiac illness, raised two first-generation children across a cultural ocean, and presented, across nearly a decade of published depiction, with no chronic diagnosis, no substance use, no somatization, and no psychiatric morbidity.

This is not invulnerability. It is a behavioral phenotype: religious practice as ritualized stress-discharge, household routine as exposure pacing, the kitchen as both vocation and biofeedback loop, and a marriage that functions as durable co-regulation. The body is maintained the way the household is maintained — by **daily, unspectacular, non-negotiable practice**.

The two things a complete file would watch for in the next decade of her depicted life: (a) delayed cardiovascular emergence in the bereavement tail, and (b) the eventual structural challenge of widowhood, should Yusuf's cardiac trajectory progress. Neither is in the record. Both are in the actuarial near-field.

*End Section 2. Cross-reference §3 (Psychological) for the affect-regulation architecture that this somatic profile rests on, and §5 (Personality) for the operational code that keeps the architecture upright.*


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — MUNEEBA KHAN

*Classification: Stage-Two Behavioral Dossier, Physical Register. Inferences derived from depicted body-language across the Wilson, Ahmed, and post-resurrection runs; gaps filled by longitudinal pattern-extrapolation.*

---

## 1. BUILD, FRAME, AND BASELINE CARRIAGE

Subject is a woman of medium height (estimated 5'4"–5'5") and a build best described as *settled* rather than soft — the body of someone who has carried two pregnancies to term, has not pursued exercise as a discipline, and has done two decades of continuous domestic labor (lifting laundry baskets, kneading dough, hauling groceries up the porch steps of the Jersey City row-house). The musculature in her forearms and shoulders is more developed than her overall silhouette suggests; this is the signature of habitual rolling, kneading, and stirring.

**Resting posture, standing:** weight evenly distributed, feet near-parallel and shoulder-width or slightly narrower, hands most often clasped at waist-height in front of her body (right over left) or resting on the back of a chair. She does not lean on door frames; she does not slouch against counters. Her spine carries a slight forward-set in the upper thoracic — the early stage of the kyphosis common in women who spend years bent over stoves, sewing machines, and small children — but she actively corrects it when she notices, lifting her sternum in a small, characteristic upward tug.

**Resting posture, seated:** ankles crossed, never knees; knees together; skirt or kameez tugged smooth across the lap with both hands as she sits down — a single fluid motion executed without looking. On the family sofa she occupies the same end-cushion consistently (left, nearest the kitchen sight-line). At the dining table she sits at Yusuf's right.

**Gait:** unhurried, deliberate, audible — she wears slip-on house sandals indoors and low block-heel pumps outdoors, and the heels click in a steady 4/4 the household uses as an early-warning system. Stride length is short. She does not swing her arms much; the upper body remains relatively still over a moving pelvis. When she is carrying something hot from stove to table she walks faster but with an even shorter stride and the elbows clamped to the ribs. When she is angry she walks *more slowly*, not less — the cadence becomes ceremonial, and household members read the slow approach as worse news than the fast one.

---

## 2. THE FACE

**Resting face:** mouth in a soft neutral line, lips closed, lower lip slightly fuller than the upper, the corners pulled neither up nor down. The default expression reads to outsiders as mildly stern; the family knows it as her *thinking* face. Eyebrows are full, naturally arched, threaded (not waxed, not plucked) every three to four weeks at a Pakistani salon on Kennedy Boulevard. Forehead is largely unlined except for a single vertical crease between the brows that deepens visibly under concentration or displeasure — the household tell that informs Kamala, Aamir, and Yusuf in roughly that order whether the conversation is about to turn.

**Eye behavior:** dark brown, deep-set, with the slight downturn at the outer corner that makes her resting expression read as appraising. She does not break eye contact first in disagreements — a learned habit from her own mother, transmitted as a marker of moral authority. With Yusuf she holds eye contact longer than with anyone else and softens at the outer corner when she does. With her children she uses the *long held look* as a discipline tool: a three- to five-second uninterrupted regard that produces compliance more reliably than any verbal instruction. With strangers and shopkeepers she breaks first, politely, after the appropriate beat.

**Blink rate** rises perceptibly when she is being lied to — not because she is processing harder, but because she is suppressing a verbal interruption. Kamala, after sixteen years, has not consciously identified this tell but reflexively shortens her lies in response to it.

**Smile architecture:** three distinct smiles, deployed by context.
- The *social smile* — closed-lipped, symmetric, brief, eyes uninvolved. Used at the door, with delivery drivers, at PTA, with Auntie Ruby.
- The *amused smile* — closed-lipped but asymmetric, the left corner pulling higher, accompanied by a single small exhale through the nose. This is her dry register, the one Kamala routinely fails to notice.
- The *full smile* — teeth showing, eye-corners crinkling, occasionally a soft laugh from the chest. Reserved for Yusuf, for her children at private domestic moments (Kamala dressed for Eid, Aamir's wedding, the first time she held Tyesha's hand), and for very small children encountered in any setting.

She does not smile while listening to other people speak unless they say something funny. The American habit of continuous reassurance-smiling she finds slightly distrustful and does not reciprocate.

**Mouth/jaw tells:** when displeased, she presses her lips inward in a small, almost imperceptible roll — the lipstick disappears for a half-second. When deeply upset, the jaw sets and the muscle at the angle of the mandible becomes visible. She does not bite her lip, does not chew the inside of her cheek, does not pick at her lips. There is no oral fidgeting in her repertoire.

---

## 3. HANDS, GESTURE, AND FINE MOVEMENT

Muneeba's hands are the most expressive part of her body — far more than her face — and a competent surveillance read of her state depends on them more than on any other channel.

**Hand baseline:** medium-sized, square-palmed, short clean nails kept filed to a soft oval and unpainted except for occasional henna on Eid and at weddings. The skin of the hands is older than the skin of the face by perhaps a decade — water-roughened across the knuckles, faintly callused at the base of the right thumb (knife work), with a small healed burn scar on the inside of the left forearm from a long-ago oil splash. Wedding band on the left ring finger (gold, simple), a thin gold bangle on the right wrist worn continuously since her own wedding, and on Fridays and Eids a second matched bangle on the left.

**Gestural repertoire:**
- *The smoothing motion:* she smooths fabric — her own dupatta across her chest, a tablecloth, a child's collar, the corner of a prayer rug — as a self-regulatory gesture roughly every four to six minutes of waking domestic time. It is not anxious; it is the somatic equivalent of a pianist running a scale.
- *The wrist-rotation:* while listening, she will slowly rotate her right wrist, making the bangle slide a half-inch up and back down. This is her thinking-gesture and a reliable indicator that she is composing a response rather than reacting.
- *The flat palm down:* used to end a conversation. Palm laid flat on the kitchen table or counter, fingers spread, a single short press. After this gesture no further argument is permitted.
- *The two-handed cup:* when delivering food, condolences, or instruction to someone she loves, she will briefly cup their face, or their hands inside her two hands, or the back of their head — a transferred physical blessing that is almost liturgical in its brevity.
- *The pointing index:* used only in rebuke, and only to children or to inanimate offenders (a stain, a misplaced shoe). She does not point at adults; she finds it discourteous.

**She does not gesticulate while speaking** in the broad American manner. Her hands stay near her body, often clasped, and accompany speech with small, low-amplitude movements at the level of the sternum.

**Fidgeting:** essentially absent at baseline. Under stress, a single tell — she will turn her wedding band twice around her finger with the thumb of the same hand, then stop. Two turns. Always two. Under acute distress (Yusuf's cardiac event, the night of Kamala's death), the count goes to three or four and the breath audibly changes on the fourth.

---

## 4. VOICE, BREATH, AND VOCAL TICS

Mezzo register, slightly nasal in Urdu, very slightly accented in English with the specific Karachi-educated softening of the t's and d's. She code-switches mid-sentence with her children, mid-clause sometimes — Urdu for the emotional core of a sentence, English for its logistical scaffolding.

**Volume:** moderate-low at baseline. She does not raise her voice. The household's most-quoted maxim about her is that *the quieter she goes, the worse it is.* True anger is delivered in something close to a whisper.

**Cadence:** measured, with full stops where Americans would have commas. She is comfortable with pauses and does not fill them with *um* or *like*. The pause itself is a rhetorical instrument.

**Verbal tics:**
- *Beta* (child) — terminal endearment, used with both Aamir and Kamala, frequency stable across moods; its absence in a sentence directed at one of her children is itself the warning.
- *Hai Allah* — the standard small-exhalation under mild frustration, deployed perhaps a dozen times a day around stove, laundry, and news broadcasts.
- *Astaghfirullah* — reserved for genuine moral offense, deployed perhaps weekly.
- *MashaAllah* — reflexive after any compliment, her own or another's, to a child.
- *"And then?"* — her standard prompt to keep a hesitant speaker (usually Kamala) talking. Delivered in a flat, patient register.

**Laughter:** low in the chest, brief, three to four pulses. She covers her mouth with her right hand when laughing fully — a learned modesty gesture from her own girlhood that she has not unlearned.

**Breath:** at baseline, slow diaphragmatic, audible only in the silence of late-night kitchen cleanup. Under stress the breath rises into the upper chest and becomes shallower; under grief it becomes irregular but does not become a sob — she breathes through grief with a closed mouth, nostrils flaring slightly, until she is alone.

---

## 5. GROOMING, DRESS, AND MAINTENANCE RITUAL

**Hair:** waist-length, dark brown going to grey at the temples (she does not dye it, and Yusuf has been politely told twice that she will not be persuaded). Braided in a single thick plait for sleep and around the house; pinned up under hijab outdoors. Washed twice a week with mustard oil massaged in the night before — a ritual she performs Thursday evenings with the radio on.

**Hijab:** worn in any space where non-mahram men might enter, including her own front porch and any view from the street. At-home she wears a loose dupatta draped over the head and shoulders, ready to be drawn fully across at the doorbell. The hijab-pin (small, plain, silver) is kept in a specific dish on the entry console; if it is not in the dish, the household is alerted that she is preparing to leave.

**Dress:** at home, shalwar kameez in soft cottons, predominantly mid-tone solids — sage, dusty rose, navy, ivory — with embroidered trim for occasions. She does not wear Western clothing. For grocery runs and parent-teacher conferences, the kameez is a darker, plainer cut; for the masjid or community gatherings, the kameez is finer and the dupatta is matched. She owns perhaps fifteen kameezes in active rotation, laundered and pressed on Sundays. Shoes off at the door, always, with a small head-tilt down-and-left as she steps out of them — a movement Kamala has unconsciously copied.

**Scent:** rosewater on the wrists in the morning; cardamom and onion in the hair by evening; faint trace of *attar* (a specific oud-and-rose blend in a small glass vial inherited from her own mother) only on Fridays and Eids. She does not wear perfume in the American sense.

**Cosmetics:** kohl along the inner waterline, applied with a small wooden stick from a tiny brass pot, every morning before fajr or shortly after. Lipstick (a single muted berry tone) for outings. No foundation, no eyeshadow, no mascara. A small bottle of Pond's cold cream on the bathroom shelf, used nightly.

**Nails, skin, teeth:** trimmed Sunday evenings. Skin oiled (almond) after the evening shower. Teeth brushed twice daily with the addition of a miswak stick used after Friday prayers.

---

## 6. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Bedtime:** 10:30–11:00 p.m., after the kitchen is fully reset for morning and the doors checked twice (front, then back, then front again — the second front check is the tell). She prays Isha last thing.

**Sleep position:** right side, knees slightly drawn, right arm under the pillow, left arm across the abdomen. She sleeps facing Yusuf. If he is restless (more frequent since the cardiac event), she will turn to face the other way and place a hand backward against his thigh — a contact bridge maintained without visual confirmation.

**Sleep depth and continuity:** historically a sound sleeper; post-cardiac-event and post-Kamala's-death, sleep has become interrupted. She wakes at roughly 3:00 a.m. for tahajjud prayer on perhaps four nights a week, returning to bed for ninety minutes before fajr.

**Wake:** 5:00–5:30 a.m. depending on season for fajr. Out of bed in a single movement, sitting up first, swinging both legs together, feet finding slippers without looking — slippers always at the same spot. She does not snooze. She does not lie in bed scrolling. The first ten minutes of her day are wudu, prayer, and the boiling of water.

**Naps:** rare, fifteen to twenty minutes on the sofa with the dupatta pulled across her eyes, only on Saturday afternoons.

**Sleep dress:** long cotton nightgown in winter, lighter cotton kameez in summer, hair plaited, no head covering. The body she presents in sleep is the most unguarded body in her repertoire.

---

## 7. EATING

**Pattern:** three meals plus afternoon tea, eaten at consistent times (breakfast 6:45, lunch 1:00, tea 4:30, dinner 7:30). She eats more slowly than anyone else at the table and is the last to finish. She serves others before herself; she serves herself last and least.

**Mechanics:** right hand for eating, by hand when the meal is roti-and-curry, by fork-and-spoon (never knife, except for cutting children's food) when the meal is Western. She tears roti with the thumb and first two fingers of the right hand in a small precise motion. She does not lick her fingers; she wipes them on a cloth napkin folded on her lap.

**Preferences:** strong tea (black, with milk and cardamom and two sugars at breakfast, one sugar at tea-time), little appetite for sweets except on Eid and at weddings, moderate spice tolerance, dislike of raw onion. She drinks water with meals, not before or after.

**Fasting:** Ramadan observed in full; she also fasts the six days of Shawwal and Mondays/Thursdays in some weeks. Her body has been habituated to monthly fasting cycles for decades; she does not become irritable or low-energy through them and continues her full domestic load.

**Stress-eating:** absent. Under stress her appetite drops; she will skip her own meal while still cooking for everyone else. Yusuf is the one who notices and quietly insists.

---

## 8. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE-PHYSICAL REGISTER

The published record offers (appropriately) no explicit material; inferences here are structural and based on the observed marital depiction.

The marriage to Yusuf is depicted as warm, partnered, and physically affectionate in the small, daily-life register — a hand on the small of his back as she passes behind him in the kitchen, a brief shoulder-touch when handing him his tea, her dupatta adjusted by his hand at the doorway before guests. They share a bedroom, a bed, and the somatic intimacy of long marriage; the depicted public modesty (no kissing or embracing in front of the children) is cultural and does not reflect the private register, which is inferable as continuingly affectionate.

Her physical reserve in public is total. She does not touch non-mahram men, will not shake hands across the gender line, and manages this with a small palm-to-chest gesture and a slight bow that conveys greeting without contact. With women in her community she is warmly tactile — kisses on both cheeks at greetings, hand-holding while seated, the long hug at departures.

With her children: physical affection is more frequent and more uninhibited than her early-era disciplinary register suggests. She kisses the tops of their heads when they sit and she stands behind. She palms their cheeks. She tucks Kamala's hair behind her ear with the back of her knuckle. Under genuine distress (the *Last Days* arc, the hospital scenes, the grief arcs) she holds them with both arms and the full length of her torso — the maternal embrace that Kamala will associate with safety for the rest of her depicted life.

---

## 9. MICRO-MOVEMENTS BY STATE

A surveillance read will distinguish her states primarily by hand and breath rather than face. Schematic:

**Calm/baseline:** breath slow and low; hands clasped or occupied; bangle silent; brow smooth; one of the three smile-forms cycling appropriately to context; voice at moderate-low volume; gait measured. The smoothing-gesture every four to six minutes.

**Mild displeasure:** vertical brow-crease deepens; lips press inward in the half-second roll; voice drops *slightly* in volume; speech rate slows; the *beta* may be omitted from the next sentence. Hands move to the hips or to the back of a chair. Smoothing-gesture frequency rises.

**Sustained displeasure / cold withdrawal (her primary discipline):** voice flattens to its lowest register; eye contact lengthens and becomes appraising; she physically turns a quarter-angle away from the offending child while continuing to address them, denying full face. She continues domestic activity with notably increased precision — the chopping becomes more rhythmic, the folding more exact. This is the worst weather in the house and the children know it.

**Acute stress / threat to a loved one:** breath rises into the upper chest; the wedding band turns twice; the bangle is rotated; the jaw sets. *And then the register flips* — under genuine catastrophe she drops the control register entirely, body softens, arms come up and out, she moves *toward* the threatened person at speed, and the voice becomes audibly tender. This inversion is the most important somatic fact in her file: her ceiling state is not rage but open, embodied tenderness, and it is reliably triggered by real (as opposed to anticipatory) danger.

**Grief:** mouth-closed, nostrils flaring; breath irregular but contained; no public weeping; the bangle is held still by the opposite hand rather than rotated. She seeks a private room — typically the bathroom or her own bedroom — and weeps there with the door closed and the tap running. After the private weep she washes her face, performs wudu, and returns. The household learns to read the slightly-pink rim of her lower eyelid as the post-grief tell.

**Joy:** the full smile; the laugh from the chest; both hands rising briefly to cup a face or the air in front of one; a small *MashaAllah* under the breath. Joy is the rarest depicted state and the one in which she most resembles the young woman she was before immigration.

**Prayer:** the most regular state-shift in her day, occurring five times. The body becomes ceremonial — measured, exact, oriented. Breath slows to its deepest register. The face goes still and the brow-crease disappears. The somatic baseline she returns to after each salat is detectably lower-arousal than the one she left.

**Intimacy with Yusuf (depicted, non-sexual register):** shoulders drop a visible half-inch; she leans the crown of her head against his shoulder when seated next to him on the sofa; her right hand finds his left forearm and rests there; her voice drops into Urdu by default. This is the only state in which she allows herself to be physically supported by another adult.

---

## 10. THE ENVELOPE OF HABITS — LONGITUDINAL CONSTANTS

Across thirty years of inferable marital and maternal life, the following have not been depicted to vary: the 5 a.m. wake; the kohl-stick; the two door-checks at night; the right-side sleep position; the Thursday hair oil; the Sunday laundry-and-nails; the Friday *attar*; the eating-last; the cooking-while-grieving; the slow-walk-when-angry; the two-turn wedding-band tell; the cupping of beloved faces with both hands. These are the spine of the somatic file — the constants against which any deviation should be read as significant.

The Khan file's central somatic finding is consistent with the psychological one: this is a body organized around containment, ritual, and the small daily transmission of care through touch and food. The container has held. The hands have not stopped moving. The kitchen light comes on at 5:15 every morning, and the kettle goes on within ninety seconds.

*End Somatic Atlas. Cross-reference to §3 Psychological and §5 Personality for state-to-trait integration.*


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS — MUNEEBA KHAN

*Subsection 6 of the Stage-One Behavioral Dossier. All inferences derived from the published canon (Wilson, Alphona, Miyazawa, Ahmed, Vellani-adjacent tie-ins, the bereavement arcs, and the post-resurrection material). Where the record is silent, that silence is itself flagged.*

---

## 6.1 Foundational Attachment Schema

The most defensible classification from the available behavioral evidence is **earned secure attachment with a vigilance-tinted, culturally-organized anxious overlay**. The classification is "earned" rather than "continuous secure" because the record contains oblique, unromanticized references to her own immigration-era hardship — a journey from Karachi into a New Jersey she had to learn to read from a defensive crouch. Subjects who arrive at secure functioning through such pressure typically carry a particular signature: stable adult bonds, intact mentalization, and a chronic *low-grade scanning* for environmental threat that does not generalize into pathology. Muneeba's file matches this signature with near-textbook fidelity.

The somatic-behavioral evidence for secure base functioning is consistent across nineteen years of publication:

- Under acute existential threat (*Last Days*, the believed end of the world), she does not freeze, dissociate, or attack — she **opens her arms**. The capacity to register a loved one's terror and respond with physical comfort, *while simultaneously experiencing one's own terror*, is among the most reliable behavioral markers of an integrated attachment system. Insecure subjects under that pressure either cling parasitically or detach defensively. Muneeba did neither.
- Her marriage to Yusuf is depicted, across every writer who has touched the household, as **continuously affectionate, mutually deferential, and free of the contempt-criticism-stonewalling cascade** that would mark an insecure dyad. They negotiate; they joke; they touch in the small ways long-married partners do (a hand on the shoulder in the kitchen, prayer side-by-side). There is no behavioral evidence of avoidant withdrawal from him, no anxious surveillance of him, no use of him as a triangulation tool against the children.
- She can be **proven wrong without humiliation collapse**. When Kamala is revealed as Ms. Marvel, when Tyesha proves devout, when Aamir's beard turns out to be sincerity rather than performance — Muneeba revises her position without requiring a face-saving ritual. Subjects with fragile attachment cannot do this without an intermediating injury.

The anxious overlay is, as noted in the Stage-One workup, **targeted rather than generalized**. She does not catastrophize about Yusuf's commute, about Aamir's wanderings, about her own health. The anxiety is *daughter-shaped* and, more specifically, *American-daughter-shaped* — a parental hypervigilance organized around the specific contents she cannot herself read: high-school social hierarchies, party-circuit risks, the calculus of mixed-gender adolescent friendship, the texture of Jersey City after dark. This is acculturation anxiety, not anxious attachment in the classical sense, and it is critical to distinguish them: anxious attachment would have her clinging to Kamala for reassurance; acculturation anxiety has her *pushing rules at Kamala for the daughter's protection*. The directionality is opposite. Muneeba does not need Kamala. Muneeba is afraid for Kamala.

## 6.2 Origins: The Inferable Developmental Substrate

The record does not give us Muneeba's own mother on the page in any extended way, but there are tells. Her religious vocabulary is fluent, embodied, and not defensive — the mark of faith transmitted in childhood rather than adopted in adulthood. Her cooking repertoire is matrilineal in tone (the way she instructs Kamala in the kitchen, the half-corrections, the muscle-memory of folding samosas). Her invocations of *"what would your nani say"* and her quick deployment of community-shame levers ("Auntie Ruby will hear about this by Friday") suggest a childhood inside a tight female intergenerational lattice — grandmothers, mothers, aunts, neighbors — that functioned as a distributed attachment network. Children raised inside such lattices typically acquire **secure-but-collectivist** attachment: bonds are real, but the bonded *unit* is the extended family rather than the dyad. This explains a great deal about her later parenting:

- She does not need to be Kamala's best friend to feel she is being a good mother. The dyadic-intimacy ideal of American middle-class parenting is not her template. Her template is **fiduciary**: a mother holds the moral, cultural, and logistical line; *intimacy* is provided in part by the broader female collective (aunties, cousins, masjid women).
- This is the structural source of the great friction with Kamala, who was raised inside an American-individualist intimacy ideology and reads her mother's fiduciary stance as coldness. It is not coldness. It is a different attachment topology mistranslated across one generation of immigration.

The immigration itself almost certainly constitutes a **chronic, sub-traumatic stressor of formative consequence**. Subjects who relocate as young adults from a dense kin-network into a sparse diasporic outpost reliably develop a heightened **gatekeeping reflex** — the unconscious accounting of every threshold (door, phone, friend, food, hour of return) as a potential leak point through which the home's integrity can be compromised. Muneeba's micro-behaviors all bear this signature: she answers the door herself; she clocks the times Kamala comes home (the canon shows her awake on the couch, lights low, when Kamala sneaks back); she knows the names of every friend's parents; she will not let a guest leave the house unfed because an underfed guest is a household-reputation hazard.

## 6.3 How She Bonds

Muneeba's bonding process has a recognizable **three-phase shape**, observable in her trajectories with Tyesha, with Bruno, with Kamala's superhero-adjacent associates as they have surfaced in the household, and even with Aamir's friends:

**Phase One — Inspection.** A new entrant to the family orbit is met with formal courtesy and *active assessment*. The questions are not interrogative in tone but are diagnostically dense: family of origin, profession, neighborhood, faith practice, food preferences (which encodes class, region, and religiosity in a single answer). The new person is *fed*, because feeding is both hospitality and observation — how someone receives food, what they refuse, how they thank, reveals them. She is not cold during this phase. She is *cataloguing*. The subject often does not realize they have been assessed until the verdict is delivered (typically to Yusuf, in Urdu, in the kitchen, after the guest has left).

**Phase Two — Provisional Inclusion.** Once the initial assessment clears a minimum threshold, the new person is granted a probationary inclusion: invited back, addressed by a relational term (*beta*, *bhai*), incorporated into food allocations. Muneeba is still watching. The probation can last months or years. Bruno, for instance, occupies a multi-year probationary slot — tolerated, fed, used for errands, but not yet *family*. He earns the upgrade slowly, through demonstrated loyalty to Kamala and observable absence of disrespect.

**Phase Three — Loyal Absolutism.** Once the bond is consolidated, it is essentially unrevokable. Muneeba's loyalty to a confirmed family member is *categorical* — she will defend Tyesha against criticism from her own circle of aunties, she will absorb Aamir's underemployment without nagging him on it in public, she will not allow Yusuf's illness to be discussed outside the immediate household. The bond, once given, functions as **non-contingent**. This is the deepest and least-noticed feature of her relational system: her *gate* is slow and high, but once one is inside, one is inside without further audit.

The implication for case management: hostile actors attempting to leverage relationships against the household would find Muneeba's perimeter difficult to penetrate but, if penetrated, would be afforded an unusual depth of access through assumed trust. Her vulnerability, paradoxically, is the very absoluteness of her phase-three commitment.

## 6.4 How She Distrusts

Distrust manifests **before** disbelief. That is, Muneeba's defensive system is calibrated to detect *misalignment of character*, not factual inaccuracy. A person who lies to her about where they were last Friday is committing a smaller offense, in her schema, than a person who tells the truth about Friday but reveals through that truth that their *priorities* are wrong. Kamala learns this the hard way across the early issues: small lies provoke disproportionate consequences not because Muneeba cannot tolerate untruth but because the lie is read as evidence of a deeper misalignment Kamala has not yet disclosed.

The behavioral tells of activated distrust are subtle and consistent:

- **A reduction in food offerings.** This is the single most reliable somatic tell. Muneeba feeds people she trusts. When she is uncertain about someone, the plate arrives smaller and less often. When she actively distrusts, the kitchen is closed to them entirely — they are received in the living room and given tea only.
- **A switch from English to Urdu** in the presence of the distrusted party, particularly when speaking to Yusuf. This is partly tactical (linguistic privacy) and partly a re-anchoring gesture: she is consolidating into her primary alliance.
- **An increase in religious-formal register.** Where she might ordinarily say "come in, sit," she will instead deliver a fuller *assalamu alaikum* with a slight head incline. The formality is a distancing instrument.
- **Spatial control of the home.** Distrusted visitors are kept in the front room and not led to the kitchen. The kitchen, in her topology, is the family's interior; admission to it is a tell of granted intimacy.
- **The dispatching of small tests.** A request to "just sit with Yusuf for a minute" while she fetches something is, when she is in assessment mode, often a structured opportunity to observe how the subject behaves unsupervised.

Notably absent from her distrust repertoire: raised voices, accusations, ultimatums, theatricality. Her distrust is *quiet*, and the subject of it frequently does not know they are being weighed.

## 6.5 How She Betrays — and Whether She Does

The published record contains **no instance of Muneeba betraying a confirmed bond**. This is not a function of insufficient stress-testing; the record includes alien invasion, terminal illness, the daughter's superhero double life, the daughter's death, the daughter's posthumous outing as a mutant, and the daughter's resurrection. None of these stressors produced a betrayal beat.

The closest analog in the file is the **early-era pattern of disciplinary withdrawal** — the cold silence that follows Kamala's transgressions. To Kamala in those issues, this *reads* as betrayal: the warmth withdrawn at the moment it is most needed. From Muneeba's frame it is not betrayal but **calibrated correction** — a culturally-coded discipline tool meant to communicate the seriousness of the breach without escalation to physical or verbal violence. The intent is pedagogical; the impact is wounding. This gap between intent and impact is the single most reliable source of mother-daughter rupture across the entire run, and it is critical to read it accurately: Muneeba does not stop loving Kamala during these silences. She is exercising the only escalation tool her tradition has authorized for non-violent serious-message delivery. That Kamala experiences it as withdrawal of love is a translation failure across generational and cultural registers, not an actual withdrawal.

The structural inference: **Muneeba is constitutionally near-incapable of strategic betrayal.** Her moral self-concept will not metabolize it. The behavior that *looks* like betrayal in her file is always one of two things: (a) disciplinary withdrawal that she does not register as betrayal, or (b) the small concealments of a parent managing a child's emotional load (not telling Kamala the full extent of Yusuf's cardiac risk, not telling Kamala she knows about Ms. Marvel until the moment of disclosure). Both are mother-protective rather than self-interested, and neither would satisfy a clinical definition of relational betrayal.

## 6.6 How She Repairs

Repair behavior is **prompt, asymmetric, and largely non-verbal**. Muneeba does not typically apologize in words. Her apology-equivalents are:

- **A plate of food, brought without comment.** The plate is the apology. The plate communicates: *I have thought about you; I have done labor on your behalf; the table is open.*
- **A physical proximity gesture** — sitting on the edge of the bed during a homework session, smoothing Kamala's hair while she is on the phone, the brief pressed-palm-to-cheek that the canon depicts at several inflection points.
- **A re-narration of the conflict** in which she gives ground without ever announcing she is giving ground. ("You know, when I was your age...") This is the closest she comes to a verbal apology — a soft autobiographical opening that signals revision of her position.
- **A delegated message.** Where she cannot say something directly, she will say it to Yusuf in Kamala's hearing, or to Aamir to deliver. The information arrives; the dignity is preserved.

Direct verbal repair, when it does occur, is **understated to the point of seeming insufficient** to a non-attuned observer. The *Last Days* and *Ms. Marvel* #19 beats are the canonical exceptions: under sufficient stakes, she can be plain. *"I knew."* *"I am proud."* The economy of those statements is itself a relational tell — she does not believe important things require many words, and she trusts the listener to receive the full freight of a short sentence. With Kamala, this trust is sometimes misplaced; Kamala wants the long version. Muneeba does not give it. The short version is, for her, more honest.

Repair is also **frequently pre-emptive**. She often initiates the next morning's normality before the prior night's rupture has been verbally addressed at all — breakfast on the table, lunchbox packed, the day resumed. This is not avoidance; it is a culturally-coded *we are still a family* signal that resets the relational state without requiring the child to perform contrition.

## 6.7 Intimacy

Intimacy, for Muneeba, is **chronically under-verbalized and structurally over-performed**. She expresses love through:

- **Provisioning** — food, clean clothes, prepared lunches, the textbook left on the desk before the test, the prayer mat unrolled. The household's logistics are her love language.
- **Anticipation** — she is observed throughout the canon to *know what the family needs before they ask*, including Kamala's emotional state on entry (the canon shows her clocking Kamala's face the moment she walks in the door and adjusting her own demeanor accordingly).
- **Prayer offered on behalf of the beloved** — she prays *for* her family in their presence, which is among the more intimate gestures her tradition affords. Kamala in the *Last Days* arc receives this directly.
- **The small touch** — brief, deliberate, not effusive. A hand on the back of the head, a thumb to the forehead, a palm on the shoulder. The duration is short, the placement consistent, the meaning unambiguous to a recipient who has been raised in the vocabulary.

Verbal expressions of love are rare and high-impact when they occur. The *"I am proud of you"* in #19 is canonically a milestone because it is rare, not because the love it expresses is novel. The love was always there; the speech act was withheld until the moment justified it.

## 6.8 Dependency

Muneeba's dependency profile is **counter-dependent in self-presentation, interdependent in actual structure**. She presents to the household and the community as the one who *holds*, never the one who *needs* — she does not ask Kamala for emotional support, does not lean on Aamir, does not burden Yusuf with her fears about his own illness. Yet the structural reality is that she is woven into a thick interdependence with Yusuf in particular: their decisions are jointly made, their finances are jointly managed (with her doing the day-to-day arithmetic), and her steadiness is observably dependent on his presence. The cardiac arc places this dependency under stress and reveals it; her competence during that period is purchased at a cost the record does not let her fully voice.

She does not depend on her children, and this is a critical distinction. **She is not the kind of immigrant mother who has fused her identity to her offspring's success or proximity.** Aamir's underachievement does not destabilize her self-concept; Kamala's heroism does not aggrandize it. Her self is anchored in her marriage, her practice, and her role within her community — not in her children's outputs. This grants the children, paradoxically, more room to fail than they realize they have.

The narrowest point of her dependency network is **her own peer intimacy**. The canon shows her with Auntie Ruby and the masjid circle, but the relationships read as sociable rather than confiding. There is no depicted close female friend to whom Muneeba *unburdens*. The unburdening, to the extent it happens, goes to Yusuf and to God. This is a structural vulnerability the file should flag: should Yusuf predecease her, her confiding network would contract to prayer alone. The bereavement arc gives us a preview of how that contraction would look — controlled, functional, internally devastating, externally legible only to the most attuned observer.

## 6.9 The Relational Template, Repeated

Across every relationship in the file — Yusuf, Aamir, Kamala, Tyesha, Bruno, Auntie Ruby, the masjid women, Kamala's later superhero-adjacent contacts when they breach the household — the same **operational template** repeats:

1. **Initial formal courtesy paired with covert assessment.** No one walks into Muneeba's orbit without being read.
2. **Provisional inclusion via food and address-terms.** The kitchen and the relational vocabulary are her gating instruments.
3. **A probationary period of observation under low-stakes interaction**, during which the subject's character is sampled across multiple contexts.
4. **A consolidation event** — usually small, often a moment of demonstrated loyalty, faith, or integrity that resolves her assessment.
5. **Categorical loyal inclusion**, after which the subject receives the full benefit of her protection, her defense in their absence, and her structural prioritization.
6. **Discipline-by-withdrawal when the included party transgresses**, calibrated to the severity of the breach and almost never escalating to direct verbal confrontation.
7. **Non-verbal repair within twenty-four hours** of any rupture that did not involve a foundational moral breach.
8. **Revision of position on evidence**, delivered without ceremony, often the deepest gift she offers — the willingness to be *wrong about you* and to say so by changing her behavior.

The template is **remarkably stable across nineteen years of publication and at least four primary writers**. That stability is itself diagnostic: it indicates a character whose relational system is not a stylistic accident of one writer but a coherent internal architecture that successive writers have been able to extend without contradiction. The file should treat her relational behavior as **highly predictable** — which is, for an intelligence dossier, the most valuable property a subject's relational system can have. Muneeba Khan, in any future scenario, will run this template again. The contents will vary. The shape will not.

*End §6. Proceed to §7: Daily Habits, Rituals, and Somatic Micro-Patterns.*


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DOSSIER SECTION — DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS
### Subject: Muneeba Khan
*Cross-reference: §3 Psychological, §5 Personality. This section disassembles the defensive architecture into its discrete components, ranks them by developmental primitiveness (Vaillant's hierarchy, modified for cultural context), and traces each through observable behavioral signatures across the published record.*

---

## I. ARCHITECTURAL OVERVIEW

Muneeba's defensive system is unusually **coherent** — that is, the mechanisms do not war with one another or produce the contradictory presentations typical of fragmented defensive structures. They operate as a stacked, layered apparatus, with mature defenses doing the bulk of the daily work, neurotic defenses activated under role-strain (specifically maternal role-strain), and primitive defenses essentially absent from the record. The system is held together by a **superordinate religious-cultural framework** that functions less as a defense in itself than as the *operating system* on which the defenses run — providing language, ritual, and causal explanation for affect that the defenses then route, contain, or discharge.

The system has one notable **structural vulnerability**: it is heavily dependent on her ability to *act* — to cook, to enforce, to manage, to provision. When agency is foreclosed (her daughter's death, her husband's cardiac event, the Incursion), the mature defenses temporarily yield to a brief, contained regression toward more primitive containment (silence, ritual repetition, physical clinging), after which the mature stack reasserts. This is not pathological; it is the system functioning as designed under loads beyond ordinary parameters.

---

## II. MATURE DEFENSES (Primary, ego-syntonic, adaptive)

### 1. **Suppression** — the load-bearing defense

This is the single most-deployed mechanism in the file and the one that gives Muneeba her characteristic public affect: composed, present, slightly remote. **Suppression is conscious or semi-conscious postponement of affect**, distinct from repression (unconscious banishment). Muneeba *knows* she is angry, frightened, or grieving; she chooses not to discharge it in the moment, and she returns to it later, often in solitary prayer or in the kitchen.

Behavioral signatures:
- The Wilson-run pattern of receiving bad news (Kamala's lies, Aamir's deepening religiosity, Tyesha's introduction) with a beat of stillness, a single short verbal response, and a redirection to a practical task ("eat your dinner," "we will discuss this later," "go to your room").
- The cardiac-event sequence with Yusuf: she does not collapse in the hospital; she manages paperwork, then prays at home alone.
- The bereavement arc: public composure at the janazah, private devastation. No witnessed scene of public breakdown is depicted; this is character-consistent suppression, not authorial omission.

The cost of suppression is delayed processing — the file repeatedly shows her returning to a topic days or weeks later with a fully-formed considered position, indicating she does the affective work *off-camera*, on her own timeline.

### 2. **Sublimation** — into nurturance and provisioning

Affect is routed into **food, household maintenance, and the physical care of others**. The kitchen is her primary site of sublimation; cooking is depicted as her default response to family stress, with the meal serving as both apology and assertion. When she cannot say "I love you and I am terrified for you," she puts a plate in front of the person. The grief arc intensifies this — the post-mortem panels showing her at the stove are doing defensive work, not merely scene-dressing.

Secondary sublimation channels: laundering Yusuf's medications into a structured pill-organizer ritual; the meticulous management of Aamir's wedding logistics; the maintenance of the home as a presentable space ready to receive community at any hour. Each is hostility, fear, or grief converted into productive provision.

### 3. **Anticipation** — the immigrant-parent calibration

Muneeba thinks forward. The hypervigilance read as anxiety in the early issues is more accurately **anticipatory defense**: she pre-imagines worst-case social, religious, and physical outcomes for Kamala, then constructs preemptive rules to forestall them. This is mature defense work, not pathology — she mentally rehearses bad futures, develops contingency plans, and absorbs the anxiety in the planning rather than carrying it as free-floating dread.

The clearest demonstration is the Ms. Marvel reveal: she had been *anticipating* the conversation, possibly for months, and arrived at it with a prepared position (pride, acceptance, continued enforcement of normal-life scaffolding). She did not improvise.

### 4. **Altruism** — bounded, in-group

A genuine mature defense in her file, though narrower than the textbook form: her own anxiety and grief are partially metabolized through **service to others within concentric rings** (family → masjid community → ummah more broadly). The reach is limited — she is not a stranger-altruist — but within her rings, the service is consistent, ungrudging, and visibly regulating for her.

### 5. **Humor** — dry, sparing, often missed

The file documents a **subtle, deadpan humor register** that the household — particularly Kamala in her adolescent phase — frequently fails to register. This is mature defense functioning: the capacity to hold a difficult situation at sufficient cognitive distance to find its absurdity, without contempt or dismissal. The humor is almost never barbed at her children; it is more often directed at the gap between immigrant expectation and American reality, or at the small comedies of community life. Its sparing use is itself diagnostic — humor is rationed, deployed when affect has already been suppressed and intellectualized, as a final small release valve.

---

## III. NEUROTIC DEFENSES (Secondary, ego-dystonic when surfaced, role-bound)

### 6. **Reaction formation** — strictness as inverted tenderness

The central neurotic mechanism in the file, and the one responsible for the entire mother-daughter conflict of Era One. The unbearable affect is *the intensity of her love and fear for Kamala*; the observable behavior is **coldness, rule-enforcement, and emotional distance**. The Last Days arc empirically demonstrates the inversion: under conditions where reaction formation is no longer needed (the world is ending; performance of distance has no remaining purpose), the underlying affect surfaces immediately and without transition. The tender mother was always there; the strict mother was the defensive overlay.

This is *neurotic* rather than mature because it produces real cost — the rupture with Kamala across adolescence is its bill — and because Muneeba is not fully conscious of the mechanism. She experiences her strictness as duty, not as defense.

### 7. **Intellectualization through religious framework**

Affect is **routed through theological vocabulary** that gives it structure and reduces its rawness. Grief becomes "Allah's plan"; fear becomes "tawakkul" (reliance); pride becomes "blessing"; anger becomes "concern for the akhirah." This is genuine intellectualization in the Vaillantian sense — the affect is real, but it is processed through an abstracting frame that buffers immediate impact.

Critically, this is *not* religious bypassing. Muneeba does not use religious language to *avoid* the feelings; she uses it to *contain and name* them so that she can sit with them. The distinction matters: bypassing would predict reduced engagement with the affect's object; her engagement is, if anything, deepened by the religious framing.

### 8. **Displacement** — minor, onto the community-gossip register

A documented but minor mechanism: Muneeba sometimes redirects anxiety about her own family onto **scenarios involving community perception** ("what will Auntie Ruby say?"). The actual fear is internal (am I failing as a mother?); the displaced expression is external (will the community see me as failing?). This is the mechanism Kamala instinctively learned to avoid triggering, because it produces disproportionate reaction relative to the underlying offense.

### 9. **Isolation of affect** — situational

Periodically, particularly around Yusuf's medical management, Muneeba demonstrates the capacity to **separate the cognitive content of a frightening situation from its emotional charge** in order to function. She can discuss cardiac risk, medication schedules, and dietary restriction in flat clinical register. The affect is not gone; it is bracketed for retrieval later. This shades into suppression but is distinguishable by its more surgical, situation-specific quality.

### 10. **Undoing** — ritual-mediated

Minor and culturally normative: the post-conflict tea, the extra serving of food after a harsh word, the small gesture that *restores* without explicitly *apologizing*. Muneeba almost never offers a verbal apology to her children; she offers undoing behaviors that accomplish the same relational repair through action rather than admission. This is neurotic because it allows her to avoid the ego-cost of explicit apology while still restoring the relationship.

---

## IV. PRIMITIVE DEFENSES (Largely absent; brief situational appearances only)

This is where Muneeba's file is most distinctive: the primitive defenses are **conspicuously underused**.

### 11. **Splitting** — *absent in any sustained form*

She does not divide people into wholly good and wholly bad. Tyesha begins as suspect and becomes embraced — without Muneeba ever having to revise a prior demonization, because she never demonized. Her initial coolness was reservation, not splitting. Similarly, her American neighbors are treated as differently-cultured but not as enemies. The absence of splitting is one of the strongest arguments for the §3 reading of earned secure attachment.

### 12. **Projection** — *minimal*

She does not attribute her own forbidden affects to others. She owns her fear, her disappointment, her pride.

### 13. **Denial** — *briefly, around Yusuf's mortality*

The one documented near-instance of primitive denial is her early-stage minimization of the severity of Yusuf's cardiac condition — a brief refusal to fully integrate the implication of his fragility. It is short-lived and yields to anticipatory and management behavior within the same arc.

### 14. **Regression** — *acute and brief, post-bereavement*

After Kamala's death, the published material shows a contained regression to **ritual repetition and physical/somatic withdrawal** — silence, reduced range, near-mutism in certain panels. This is regression in the technical sense (return to earlier modes of self-soothing), but it is bounded, time-limited, and does not impair functioning past the acute window. The mature stack reasserts.

### 15. **Somatization** — *absent*

Notable for its absence. A subject with this affective load and this much suppression would, in many clinical pictures, present somatic symptoms (headaches, GI distress, fatigue). The file shows none. This suggests the suppression is genuinely *suppressive* (conscious deferral) rather than *repressive* (unconscious banishment with somatic return).

---

## V. COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — POSITIVE

These are not defenses proper but **structured behaviors that offset the costs of the defensive stack** and maintain overall functioning.

### a. **Religious practice as integrative ritual**
Five daily prayers, Quranic recitation, fasting, communal worship. These provide:
- **Time-structuring** that prevents grief or anxiety from colonizing all hours;
- **Embodied affect-regulation** via the physical movements of salah (prostration as parasympathetic activation);
- **Linguistic containers** (du'a) for affect that has no other socially permissible outlet;
- **Communal reinforcement** of identity and meaning.

This is the most powerful compensatory engine in her system. Without it, the suppression-heavy defensive stack would likely accumulate cost.

### b. **The kitchen as workshop**
Cooking is both sublimation (above) and compensation: the rhythmic, sensory, generative work counterbalances the inhibitory work of suppression. It is also one of the few domains where she is uncontested authority, providing competence-affirmation that buffers maternal-role doubt.

### c. **Marriage to Yusuf as co-regulation**
The marriage is depicted as genuinely affectionate, with Yusuf's softer affective range complementing her containment. He laughs more; she manages more; they meet in the middle. The dyad functions as a mutual-regulation system in which his expressiveness gives her permission to occasionally relax containment, and her competence gives him permission to be the gentler partner.

### d. **Community embeddedness (masjid, aunties, extended family)**
Provides distributed social load-bearing — when one relationship is strained, others remain available. Reduces the catastrophic-loss potential of any single relationship (which is why Kamala's death, while devastating, does not destroy her).

### e. **Maternal identity as superordinate**
Her self-concept as Mother is large enough to absorb shocks to any sub-component (Kamala disobeys → still her daughter; Kamala is Ms. Marvel → still her daughter; Kamala is dead → still her daughter, now in different relation). The role outlives any particular state of the child.

### f. **Domestic legibility**
The home is kept ready. Tidiness, provisioning, and presentability are compensatory in the sense that they produce a **visible, controllable order** that offsets the invisible, uncontrollable disorders (her children's inner lives, her husband's health, the foreign culture outside the door).

---

## VI. COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — NEGATIVE (costs, leakages, maladaptive substitutions)

### a. **Control as proxy for connection**
The signature negative pattern of Era One. When affective access to Kamala feels uncertain, Muneeba defaults to **enforcing rules** as a substitute for inquiring into feeling. Rules feel like presence to her; to Kamala they feel like distance. This is the single largest cost the defensive stack imposes on the household, and it is the cost she eventually identifies and corrects (post-Era Three).

### b. **Community gossip as discipline lever**
The "what will Auntie Ruby say?" mechanism (see §III.8). Effective in the short term, corrosive in the long term: it teaches Kamala that performance-of-respectability matters more than authenticity, which is precisely the lesson Muneeba does *not* actually believe but reflexively transmits.

### c. **Comparison as motivator**
Episodic invocation of other families' daughters as implicit benchmarks. A mild but real maladaptive habit, particularly around academics and marriage prospects. Costs are paid in Kamala's adolescent self-esteem.

### d. **Asymmetric vigilance (gendered)**
Aamir receives lighter scrutiny than Kamala. Muneeba would, if asked, articulate a principled reason (different vulnerabilities, different cultural exposures); the behavioral pattern is nevertheless asymmetric, and the cost is paid both in Kamala's resentment and in Aamir's under-supervision during his own period of religious intensification.

### e. **Apology-avoidance via undoing**
The substitution of restorative action for verbal acknowledgment (§III.10) leaves certain relational wounds **unclosed at the linguistic level**, even when closed behaviorally. Kamala in particular benefits from words; Muneeba offers actions. The gap is a chronic, low-grade friction.

### f. **Deferred processing accumulation**
Suppression's specific failure mode: when too many items are deferred at once (Kamala's secret + Yusuf's heart + Aamir's marriage + community expectations), the queue lengthens and items can be lost — surfacing weeks later, out of context, as a sudden sharp response to a minor present trigger. The file shows occasional instances of this delayed-discharge pattern.

### g. **Refusal to burden**
She systematically declines to disclose her own distress to her children, framing it as protective. The cost is that her children consequently underestimate her interiority — they discover, repeatedly and to their own grief, that she knew more, felt more, and bore more than she ever told them. This is the defensive pattern that most resembles, in its long-term relational effects, the immigrant-parent silences documented in the broader diaspora literature.

---

## VII. INTEGRATIVE READ

The defensive architecture is, in aggregate, **the architecture of a person built to last**. It is suppression-heavy, mature-dominant, religiously scaffolded, and behaviorally productive. Its costs fall almost entirely in the **relational-disclosure domain** — what she does not say, what she does not show — and almost not at all in the functional, somatic, or psychiatric domains. The system is optimized for endurance under load and for the transmission of a moral-cultural inheritance across a generational and geographic gap; it is suboptimized for the kind of expressive emotional attunement her American-raised daughter most wanted from her.

The single most important fact about this defensive stack, for any analyst building a longitudinal model, is that **it updates**. Reaction formation yielded when its purpose was exposed. Control-as-proxy yielded when its cost was visible. The container is rigid in shape but its contents are revisable. This is the feature that distinguishes Muneeba Khan's defensive system from the brittle, similarly-structured systems that fail catastrophically under the kinds of pressure her file documents her surviving.

*End section. Cross-reference forward to §VI Habits & Rituals (granular behavioral inventory) and §VII Relational Map (dyadic patterns).*


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE — MUNEEBA KHAN

*Section 3.B of Stage-Two Dossier. Decade-by-decade clinical reconstruction. Frameworks invoked: attachment theory (Bowlby/Ainsworth/Main), Vaillant's hierarchy of defenses, Linehan's affect-regulation taxonomy, Berry's acculturation model, Erikson's psychosocial stages, Kernberg's structural interview categories, and the immigration-clinical literature on acculturation-gap distress (Suárez-Orozco; Telzer). All anchors are canonical behavior or canonically-implied biographical fact.*

---

## I. PRE-DIASPORA BASELINE — KARACHI YOUTH (inferred, c. late 1960s through 1980s)

The published record handles Muneeba's Pakistani childhood obliquely — references in *Ms. Marvel* (Wilson, 2014–2019) and in Ahmed's *Magnificent Ms. Marvel* (2019–2021) to "back home," to the way "my mother" did things, to the specific Karachi neighborhood vocabulary she still uses when speaking with Aunties — but the inferential floor is firm enough to draw.

**Affect regulation, baseline of formation:** the household of origin appears to have been one in which emotion was *expressed within ritual and contained outside it*. Her invocation of communal weeping at funerals, of celebratory loudness at weddings, alongside her own profound reticence in unstructured emotional contexts, is consistent with what cross-cultural affect researchers (Mesquita; Tsai) describe as *ideal affect calibrated to context rather than to internal state*. She did not learn — and would not later teach Kamala — that feelings are to be spoken when they arise; she learned that feelings are to be *placed* in their proper container (prayer, ritual gathering, kitchen confidence with a sister or cousin) and otherwise held.

**Cognitive style, formative:** concrete, deductive-from-principle, oriented to *hukm* (rule) rather than to *ijtihad* (independent reasoning) in domestic matters, though not doctrinaire. Her later capacity for evidence-based revision (see Eras Three and Four) suggests the formation was not authoritarian-rigid but rule-centered with a quiet pragmatism — a household where the rules were respected publicly and negotiated privately.

**Self-concept, formative:** organized around being a *good daughter*, future *good wife*, future *good mother* — a triad of role-identities pre-installed and accepted without protest in the canonical record. There is no evidence in any flashback or aside of an alternative self-narrative (artist, professional, traveler) ever having been live for her. This is not flatness; it is *fit*. She accepted the assigned identity and made it her own.

---

## II. EMIGRATION AND EARLY MARRIAGE — LATE 1980s / EARLY 1990s (Muneeba aged roughly 22–30)

Canon establishes that the Khans emigrated from Karachi to Jersey City as a young married couple, that Aamir was born in the United States (he is the elder child, in his early twenties during the Wilson run), and that the early American years were materially difficult — oblique references to Yusuf's first jobs, to a small apartment, to the building of the household.

**Affect regulation in this period:** this is the era in which her lifelong *suppression-as-mature-defense* pattern was likely *forged* rather than inherited. Vaillant's distinction matters here: suppression (the *conscious* postponement of attention to a distressing feeling) is a mature defense; repression (its unconscious cousin) is neurotic. Muneeba's adult pattern is unmistakably the former — she knows what she feels, she chooses when to feel it. That choosing is a *skill*, and skills are built under load. The load, in this period, was the standard first-generation immigrant compound: linguistic exposure, economic precarity, isolation from natal kin, the labor of building a new community from scratch (the masjid circle, the Aunties, the long-term friendships that by 2014 are decades deep). She would have had to *not* fall apart, repeatedly, in service of a husband working long hours and a small son needing stability. The capacity became characterological.
