- A standing late-Friday-evening phone call to her sister in Karachi, weekly without fail, conducted in the bedroom with the door closed.

---

## 9. THE WEEK A SURVEILLANCE TEAM WOULD ACTUALLY RECORD

Compressed: **Six wakings before dawn, thirty-five prayers, eighteen prepared meals, two grocery runs, one masjid visit, six to twelve phone calls of substance, three loads of laundry, one deep-cleaning project, one community obligation discharged, one act of charity, one extended conversation with her husband per night, two to four extracted-information exchanges with each child in residence, one serial episode watched, one chapter of Qur'an read on most days, zero raised voices except in genuine emergency, zero alcohol, zero tobacco, zero medications other than a multivitamin and whatever seasonal allergy management she requires, six to seven hours of sleep on weekdays, perhaps eight on a good Sunday.**

The file's defining observation: **she does almost exactly the same things, at almost exactly the same times, every week, and the regularity is not rigidity but architecture.** It is the structure inside which she has held a marriage, raised two children, absorbed a husband's near-death, buried and recovered a daughter, and remained — in the published record — recognizably herself. The container §3 identified is built out of these hours. A week of surveillance would not record drama. It would record the daily, repeatable construction of the thing that does not break.

*End section. Continue to next dossier component on request.*


## Relationships I — Family & Origin Bonds

# RELATIONSHIPS I — FAMILY & ORIGIN BONDS
## Subject: Muneeba Khan
*Classification: Stage-Two Relational Mapping. Each bond traced longitudinally across the published record; dynamics, escalation patterns, trust topology, and leverage points indexed per person.*

---

## 5.1 — YUSUF KHAN (Husband)

### Origin and Structural History

The marriage is the load-bearing wall of Muneeba's psychological architecture. Canonical material (Wilson run, 2014–2019; Ahmed run, 2019–2021) treats it as a settled, decades-long partnership begun in Pakistan and carried through immigration to Jersey City. Specific courtship beats are not depicted, but the texture of the marriage in published scenes — the easy code-switching between Urdu and English mid-sentence, the absence of negotiated formality, the way Yusuf finishes her stove-side instructions without looking up — is the texture of a couple who have been operationally fused for thirty-plus years. There is no canonical evidence of a prior engagement, a contested match, or in-law strain at origin.

### Dynamics

Muneeba is the household's *enforcement and logistics arm*; Yusuf is its *philosophical and emotional ballast*. Their division of labor is consistent across every issue in which they share panel-space: she sets the rule, he supplies the gentler gloss; she withdraws affection as discipline, he restores it as reconciliation. This is not a "bad cop / good cop" routine consciously deployed — it is the spontaneous equilibrium of two people whose temperaments dovetail. Muneeba does not resent Yusuf for being the softer parent. She *requires* him to be, because his softness is what makes her hardness survivable for the children, and she knows it.

Physical register: in the domestic space, she touches him casually — a hand on his shoulder when passing behind his chair, adjustments of his collar, the quiet handing-over of a teacup without verbal request. In public, she is more formal but never distant. There is no canonical depiction of overt marital conflict; disagreements, when they occur, are conducted in lowered Urdu in the kitchen and resolved before the children re-enter the room.

### Evolution

- **Pre-Reveal Era (2014–2017):** They are co-aligned on Kamala's discipline, with Yusuf occasionally functioning as quiet release valve (the famous *Ms. Marvel* #3 scene of Yusuf telling Kamala she is his "perfect little girl" is enabled by Muneeba's absence from the panel; it is not a marital fracture, it is a deliberate parental handoff).
- **Post-Reveal Era (2017–2021):** Yusuf is brought in on the Ms. Marvel knowledge later than Muneeba. Muneeba carries the secret alone for an extended period — characteristic of her containment style — and the disclosure to Yusuf is depicted as relieving rather than fraught.
- **Cardiac Event Era:** Muneeba absorbs the medical-logistical load entirely. She does not perform burden. She manages medication schedules, dietary substitution (the household's cooking shifts measurably toward low-sodium without commentary), and she begins to triage which family stressors reach Yusuf at all. This is the first canonical instance of Muneeba treating her husband as someone to be *protected from information* — a register previously reserved for the children.
- **Bereavement Era:** After Kamala's death, the marriage becomes the surviving structure. They grieve in parallel and in private; the file shows them praying together more frequently, sitting in the same room in silence more often. Neither collapses onto the other, which would be uncharacteristic of both.

### Trust and Safety

Trust is total and asymmetric only in domain, not in degree. He trusts her judgment on children, household, community standing, and money. She trusts his judgment on faith, ethics-in-the-abstract, and her own moments of overreach (he is the only person canonically depicted as able to talk her down from a disciplinary decision, and he does so by reframing rather than opposing). Safety: she is physically and emotionally safe with him in a way that frees her control mechanisms to operate elsewhere. The marriage is the place she does not have to manage.

### Failure Mode

The marriage's structural vulnerability is **Yusuf's mortality.** Muneeba's competence-as-shield strategy cannot solve cardiac disease. If Yusuf predeceases her, the file predicts a sharper psychological event than Kamala's death produced, because Kamala's death was absorbable into her existing role-scaffolding (mother-of-the-dead is a known posture in her cultural-religious vocabulary; widow is also known, but it removes the daily co-regulator). Secondary failure mode: if she ever became convinced she had failed him in some domain he cared about, the guilt would be containerless — Yusuf is the only person whose disappointment she could not metabolize through her usual frameworks.

### Leverage

To move Muneeba through Yusuf: appeals to his health, his peace, his dignity. She will concede on points she would otherwise hold if framed as protective of him. This is not manipulable by outsiders (she would detect the maneuver), but it is the lever Aamir and Kamala have both, consciously or not, used.

---

## 5.2 — KAMALA KHAN (Daughter)

### Origin and Structural History

The central relationship of the dossier. Kamala is the younger child, American-born, the locus of every acculturation anxiety Muneeba carries. From the first issue, Muneeba's behavior toward Kamala is *qualitatively different* from her behavior toward Aamir — more vigilant, more corrective, more invested. The file reads this as gendered (the cultural transmission burden falls disproportionately on daughters in her framework) and as temperamental (Kamala is the more legible-to-Muneeba child; their friction is the friction of similarity, not opposition).

### Dynamics — The Pre-Reveal Architecture

For roughly the first three years of published material, Muneeba operates a *deliberate disinformation environment* around Kamala. She knows — by her own later admission — that her daughter is Ms. Marvel "for a long time" before disclosing the knowledge. During this period, she continues to enforce curfews, police clothing, monitor friendships, and demand accountings of Kamala's whereabouts that she *knows* will be lies. This is, on its face, a baffling parenting strategy. The file's read: Muneeba was constructing a maintained surface of normalcy that allowed Kamala to retain a non-super life she could return to. The rules were *cover*, not control. She was being her daughter's alibi.

This is the single most psychologically sophisticated act in Muneeba's file, and Kamala does not perceive it as such until disclosure.

### Friction Texture

Day-to-day conflict beats — extensively cataloged across the Wilson run — include:
- Clothing: Muneeba's repeated, micro-graded corrections of Kamala's dress, calibrated to the audience (looser at mosque, more permissive at home, escalated when Bruno is present).
- Food: Muneeba's serving and her commentary on Kamala's eating are a primary nonverbal channel; refusing food in this household is a declaration, and Kamala periodically declares.
- Friends: Muneeba's vigilance about Bruno specifically (boy, non-Muslim, in Kamala's room) and Nakia approvingly (girl, Muslim, family-known).
- Phone and curfew: classic adolescent surveillance, intensified by Muneeba's *accurate* sense that Kamala is hiding something larger than typical adolescent matters.

Muneeba's primary disciplinary tool with Kamala is *cold withdrawal* — not yelling, not punishment-as-event, but the deliberate removal of warmth, the formal address, the silence at the table. Kamala finds this far more punitive than her mother's words, and Muneeba knows it.

### Evolution

- **Era One (2014–2015):** Adversarial-loving. Muneeba is the wall Kamala defines herself against.
- **Era Two (*Last Days*, 2015):** Under genuine end-of-world conditions, Muneeba abandons the wall entirely and is openly tender — physical comfort, shared prayer. Kamala sees, for perhaps the first time as a teenager, who her mother actually is underneath the role. The file marks this as the relational hinge.
- **Era Three (2017, Disclosure):** Muneeba reveals her knowledge of Kamala's identity. She offers pride rather than prohibition. The relationship reorganizes around shared secret rather than enforced ignorance.
- **Era Four (2017–2022):** Allyship-with-residual-friction. Muneeba still corrects on minor matters — driving, grades, sleep, eventual marriage prospects — but the operating mode is collaborative. She begins to be openly funny with Kamala, a register the early issues do not show.
- **Era Five (2022–2023, Death):** The loss reorganizes everything. Muneeba's grief is canonically depicted as nearly silent in public and devastating in the moments of privacy the page is permitted to witness.
- **Era Six (Resurrection/Mutant Reveal):** Acceptance-with-worry, on the original Ms. Marvel reveal template, slightly faster. Muneeba is not surprised that her daughter is more than she appeared to be; she has been surprised by Kamala her entire life.

### Trust and Safety

Trust evolves from low (era one, Kamala lies routinely, Muneeba expects it) to high (era four, Kamala discloses by default). Safety: Kamala is physically and economically safe with Muneeba throughout, and emotionally safe in proportion to her willingness to be legible. The early-era unsafety was *interpretive* — Kamala feared being seen incorrectly by her mother. The middle-era discovery was that being seen correctly was, in fact, what Muneeba had been doing all along.

### Failure Mode

The relationship's recurring failure mode is **Muneeba substituting rule-enforcement for emotional inquiry** under stress. When Muneeba is frightened by Kamala — frightened *for* her, frightened *of* losing her — her first move is to tighten the perimeter rather than ask the question. This is the pattern that drove Kamala to lie in the first place, and it is the pattern Muneeba spent years deliberately weaponizing into protective cover, but it remains the default she falls back into under acute fear.

### Leverage

What moves Muneeba in matters concerning Kamala: evidence of Kamala's competence, evidence of Kamala's faith, evidence of Kamala's safety. What does *not* work: appeals to Kamala's autonomy in the abstract. Muneeba does not grant the premise that adolescent autonomy is a value; she grants competence as it is demonstrated. The lever Kamala learned to pull — and which is now structurally available — is *honesty offered before it is demanded.* Muneeba forgives almost anything disclosed; she punishes concealment specifically.

---

## 5.3 — AAMIR KHAN (Son)

### Origin and Structural History

Older brother, devout to a degree that initially worries both parents (the early Wilson run frames Aamir's religiosity as borderline excessive in Muneeba's view — she is observant, but she is also pragmatic about American economic participation, and Aamir's refusal to work jobs he considers compromised reads to her, at first, as evasion dressed as piety). The relationship's history is the slow movement from that suspicion to active maternal advocacy.

### Dynamics

Muneeba is markedly *less surveillant* of Aamir than of Kamala. This is the file's clearest evidence of gendered parenting asymmetry. She does not police his clothing, his friendships, or his whereabouts; she critiques his employment and, occasionally, his cooking-pot-emptying. The relationship operates in a register of *exasperated affection* on her side and *deferential affection* on his. Aamir kisses his mother's hand or forehead in greeting beats; Kamala does not, and the file notes the difference as elective, not enforced.

Aamir is also the only family member who openly *defers* to Muneeba's authority on religious grounds — invoking her status as mother as theologically weight-bearing in a way Kamala and Yusuf do not. This is intermittently weaponized (Aamir invoking maternal authority to win sibling arguments) and intermittently sincere.

### Evolution

- **Early Era:** Muneeba's quiet skepticism of Aamir's choices. She defers to him publicly while privately advocating to Yusuf for a more practical son.
- **Marriage to Tyesha:** Aamir's choice of bride — a Black American convert — is the first major test of Muneeba's flexibility on community-standing matters. The initial coolness is canonical and brief. By the wedding, Muneeba is functionally integrated with Tyesha; by the post-wedding era, she advocates for Tyesha against community gossip.
- **Post-Kamala Death:** Aamir's role in the household amplifies. Muneeba leans on his religious framework for shared mourning vocabulary in a way she could not have leaned on Kamala.
- **Kamala's Mutant Status:** Aamir's response is canonically the most fraught — he struggles with the disclosure on identity-categorical grounds. Muneeba's role in this beat is mediator, which is itself notable: she has become the relationally flexible one and her son the rigid one, an inversion of the early-era configuration.

### Trust and Safety

High mutual trust, low surveillance, low conflict, low intimacy of the kind Muneeba shares with Kamala or Yusuf. Aamir is the child Muneeba does not have to *manage*, which means he is also the child she does not *know* in the same granular way. She would be the last to detect a hidden interior life in Aamir, because she has structurally stopped looking.

### Failure Mode

The under-surveillance is the failure mode in mirror to Kamala's over-surveillance. If Aamir were ever in significant trouble — spiritual, marital, financial, ideological — Muneeba's likely lag in detection would be substantial. She trusts him into invisibility.

### Leverage

To move Muneeba through Aamir: invoke his judgment, his religious standing, or his welfare. She will accept counsel from Aamir on faith-framed matters she would not accept from Yusuf. Conversely, Aamir's disappointment is a weight she would carry — though he has, in the published record, almost never offered it.

---

## 5.4 — TYESHA HILLMAN-KHAN (Daughter-in-Law)

### Origin and Structural History

Tyesha enters as Aamir's fiancée — a Black American convert to Islam, intelligent, observant, with her own family complexity. Muneeba's initial reception is canonically cool: not hostile, not racist in any explicit register, but reserved in the way she is reserved toward outsiders generally. The community-standing reflex activates; she is alert to how the marriage will read to the Auntie network.

### Dynamics and Evolution

The shift from cool reception to genuine warmth is one of the cleanest demonstrations in the file of Muneeba's capacity to *update on evidence*. The mechanism is direct exposure: Tyesha's sincerity, her religious literacy (which Muneeba can evaluate), her treatment of Aamir, and her competence as a household participant all register. Within the published arc, Muneeba moves from formal acceptance to active defense — when community gossip touches Tyesha, Muneeba is the one who shuts it down, and she does so using the same cold-withdrawal tool she uses on her children, this time deployed *protectively*.

By the later Ahmed run, Tyesha is structurally inside the household perimeter. Muneeba teaches her recipes, includes her in the women's-side conversations at family events, and treats her pregnancy (when it arrives) with full maternal-grandmaternal investment.

### Trust and Safety

Trust is moderate-high and growing. Safety is full from the Tyesha-toward-Muneeba direction. The remaining asymmetry is that Tyesha will likely never be in Muneeba's *first* circle of confidants the way Yusuf and, eventually, Kamala were — not for any deficit on Tyesha's part, but because Muneeba's first circle was sealed before Tyesha arrived.

### Failure Mode

The risk is **community-pressure regression**: if a sufficiently coordinated piece of community criticism of Tyesha emerged, the file gives moderate probability that Muneeba's first instinct would be to *manage Tyesha's presentation* before defending her outright. She would arrive at defense, but slower than Tyesha would deserve.

### Leverage

Tyesha's standing with Muneeba is durable. To move Muneeba via Tyesha: appeals to family integrity, to Aamir's happiness, or to the welfare of any grandchild. Tyesha has effective veto on questions concerning her own household that Muneeba would not extend to Kamala at equivalent age.

---

## 5.5 — THE GRANDCHILD (Aamir and Tyesha's Child)

Limited canonical material, but enough to register: Muneeba in the grandmother role is depicted as *visibly looser* than Muneeba in the mother role. The control mechanisms relax; the tenderness comes forward unmediated. This is consistent with the general grandparent literature and with the file's read of Muneeba's strictness as *role-bound rather than characterological* — when the role does not demand the wall, the wall is not built.

The grandchild also functions, post-Kamala's death and resurrection, as a continuity object: evidence that the family line and the household survive. Muneeba's investment in the grandchild is therefore overdetermined and the file flags it as a probable future psychological anchor.

---

## 5.6 — PARENTS AND SIBLINGS (Origin Family)

The published record is canonically thin on Muneeba's parents and siblings of origin. References are oblique: she came from Pakistan, immigrated with Yusuf, maintains some correspondence with extended family. There is no depicted living parent in the U.S. timeline, no depicted sibling in regular contact, and no depicted return visit of dramatic weight.

The file treats this absence as informative rather than empty: Muneeba operates without a visible parental superego figure in her American life. This is rare for a woman of her described temperament, and it likely contributes to the intensity of her *self*-imposed standards. With no living mother to defer to or rebel against, Muneeba *became* the mother — the moral-cultural authority in her household — younger and more totally than she might otherwise have. The strictness in her parenting is, in this read, partly an inheritance she is *performing without a referent*, reconstructing what her mother (or grandmother) would have done from memory, principle, and community consensus rather than from live consultation.

If extended family members surface in future canon, the file predicts Muneeba's behavior toward them will be deferential-on-form, independent-in-substance — she will offer respect ritually and decide for herself privately.

---

## 5.7 — THE DEAD: KAMALA, IN MEMORY

Kamala's death and subsequent resurrection produced a brief but psychologically permanent state in Muneeba: *mother of a dead daughter*. The resurrection does not erase the file entry; it adds to it. Muneeba has lived in the country of bereavement, and she carries the passport.

Behavior consistent with this internal state:
- A measurable increase in physical reassurance-seeking with the resurrected Kamala — small touches, the offered plate, the recurring "are you eating" interrogations now read as mortality-tracking rather than dietary policing.
- An accelerated willingness to disclose, to praise, to express directly — the bereavement compressed Muneeba's lifelong delay between feeling and saying.
- A muted, persistent vigilance around any reference to dying, danger, or absence. She does not flinch visibly; she absorbs and re-enters the room. The containment habit holds, but the contents have grown heavier.

### Failure Mode

The resurrection is a gift Muneeba accepts without theological difficulty (the family framework absorbs miracles natively), but the file flags the *next* serious threat to Kamala as the likely point at which Muneeba's containment could finally fracture. She has paid the price once; the second time may exceed her scaffolding.

### Leverage

The dead Kamala is, in a sense, a permanent third presence in every interaction Muneeba has with the living Kamala. Anyone — friend, ally, adversary — who acknowledges this without exploiting it earns a tier of credit with Muneeba that nothing else can purchase. Conversely, anyone who treats Kamala's death as past-tense will be quietly, permanently downgraded in Muneeba's estimation. This is the one matter on which she does not update.

---

*End of Section. Continues: Relationships II — Community, Faith, and Civic Bonds.*


## Relationships II — Allies, Chosen Family & Mentors

# RELATIONSHIPS II — ALLIES, CHOSEN FAMILY & MENTORS

*Subject: Muneeba Khan. Scope: every non-blood, non-nuclear human attachment of operational significance across the published record, plus the two blood-kin relationships (Aamir, Tyesha-by-marriage) that function in her psychic economy as *chosen* rather than merely given. Each entry: provenance, dynamic, evolution, trust-and-safety architecture, characteristic failure mode, and the leverage each holds — and that she holds in return.*

A preliminary note on the shape of this section. Muneeba's allyship roster is, by Western middle-class standards, *small*. She does not collect people. She does not have a confidante in the American sense — no single best friend with whom she debriefs the marriage, no therapist, no journaling practice, no book club. What she has instead is a **functional kinship lattice**: a small number of high-trust relationships organized by role (sister-of-the-faith, sister-in-law-by-affection, fellow-mother, community elder), each of whom holds a specific compartment of her inner life. No one person holds the whole. This is itself diagnostic — it is the same containment architecture that organizes her affect (§3 of the workup), externalized as a social pattern. She distributes herself in pieces so that no single rupture can collapse her.

---

## 1. AUNTIE RUBY — *the mirror, the threat, the index of community*

**Provenance.** Ruby Bashir (the surname is established only obliquely in Wilson-era backmatter and the Jersey City Masjid scenes) is a fixture of the Khan household from Kamala's earliest issues. She is not biological kin. She is the closest analogue Muneeba has to a peer-confidante, and the relationship is older than the published record — Ruby is depicted from issue one as someone whose arrival in the Khan kitchen requires no announcement and triggers no domestic reorganization. She walks in. She sits. She is given tea without asking.

**Dynamic.** This is the most *interpersonally complex* of Muneeba's relationships because it operates on two registers simultaneously. On the surface, Ruby is the gossipy Auntie — the one who reports on whose daughter was seen where, whose son is engaged to whom, whose hijab slipped at the bazaar. Muneeba participates in this exchange, sometimes appears to enjoy it, and is observably skilled at it (she gives little, extracts much, never volunteers a Khan-family vulnerability). On the deeper register, Ruby functions as Muneeba's **index of community standing** — the sensor by which Muneeba gauges how the Khan household is being perceived by the Jersey City Pakistani-American Muslim community. Ruby is, in effect, the API to public opinion.

**Evolution.** Across the Wilson run, Ruby is more often deployed as a comic figure (the lever Muneeba reaches for when disciplining Kamala — "what will Auntie Ruby say?"). Across the Ahmed run and into the bereavement arcs, Ruby's function quietly deepens: she is present at the hospital, present at the funeral, present at the post-funeral household, and — critically — she is one of the very few people in whose presence Muneeba is depicted weeping without first turning away. This is a substantial trust marker. It does not mean Ruby is loved; it means Ruby is **inside the perimeter of permissible witness**.

**Trust and safety.** Medium-high, asymmetric. Muneeba trusts Ruby with affect (post-bereavement) and with logistical/community matters; she does not trust Ruby with information. The Ms. Marvel secret, even after Muneeba herself knew it, was never shared with Ruby in any depicted scene. This is consistent with Muneeba's broader pattern: she gives Ruby the *appearance* of access while quietly compartmentalizing the operationally sensitive data.

**Failure mode.** The relationship's catastrophic failure scenario, never realized in canon but structurally available, is a **gossip leak that damages Kamala's standing or Aamir's marriage prospects**. If Ruby were ever to broadcast — even unintentionally — a household secret that produced community shame, Muneeba's response would not be confrontation; it would be a slow, polite, irrevocable cooling. She would not cut Ruby off; she would simply stop being *available* to her in the deep register. Ruby would still be served tea. She would no longer be wept in front of.

**Leverage.** Ruby holds the largest single piece of community-reputation leverage over Muneeba — she could, if she chose, materially damage the Khans' social standing. Muneeba's counter-leverage is *informational asymmetry*: Ruby tells Muneeba everything; Muneeba tells Ruby almost nothing. Ruby therefore needs Muneeba (as the sober ear, the moral arbiter, the one whose judgment she respects) more than Muneeba needs Ruby. This asymmetry is, I assess, deliberately maintained.

---

## 2. SHEIKH ABDULLAH — *the moral arbiter, the unobserved respect*

**Provenance.** The imam of the Jersey City Masjid the Khans attend. Introduced early in the Wilson run primarily through his interactions with Kamala and Bruno, and through Aamir's deeper engagement with the masjid. Muneeba's depicted interactions with him are sparse but consistently coded with a register she uses for almost no one else: *deference without diminishment*.

**Dynamic.** Sheikh Abdullah is the only figure in Muneeba's documented social field who occupies a position of **legitimate authority over her own moral self-conception**. She does not defer to Yusuf in this register (the marriage is depicted as peer-affectionate, not hierarchical-religious). She does not defer to her own mother in any on-page scene. She defers, quietly, to the Sheikh — not in a posture of submission, but in the specific posture of *consulting an expert on matters where her own judgment, however confident, is not the final word*.

**Evolution.** Across the Wilson run, the Sheikh's most consequential interaction-by-proxy with Muneeba is his initial misreading and subsequent recognition of Kamala's heroism — an arc that parallels Muneeba's own. There is, I assess, a structural sympathy between these two characters: both are figures who begin as apparent obstacles to Kamala and are progressively revealed as perceptive allies who have been quietly tracking her growth. Muneeba would not articulate this parallel. But her tone shifts toward him over the run in a way that suggests she registers it.

**Trust and safety.** High in the religious-moral domain; null in the personal-affective domain. She would consult him on whether a decision is *right*. She would not consult him on whether she is *afraid*. The compartmentalization is total and characterological — it would be a category error in her cognitive map to bring private grief to the Sheikh as grief; she would bring it as a question about practice.

**Failure mode.** The Sheikh's hypothetical failure for Muneeba would be a *public moral pronouncement she could not in conscience accept* — for instance, a ruling that condemned Kamala's heroic activity, or that delegitimized Aamir's marriage to Tyesha. In that scenario, Muneeba would not argue. She would, with the same quiet finality she would deploy against Ruby's hypothetical betrayal, **find another masjid** — and would never explain why. Her loyalty to her family supersedes her deference to clerical authority, but the supersession would be enacted by withdrawal, not by confrontation.

**Leverage.** He holds the smallest amount of leverage of anyone on this list — religious-interpretive leverage only, and she has the cultural-religious literacy to seek a second opinion. She holds even less over him; she is one congregant among many. The relationship is best characterized as *institutional* rather than personal, but it occupies a load-bearing position in her psyche because it externalizes and validates her own moral framework.

---

## 3. TYESHA HILLMAN-KHAN — *the daughter-in-law who became a daughter*

**Provenance.** Aamir's wife. Black American convert to Islam. Introduced in the Wilson run during Aamir's marriage arc; their relationship is, in the published record, one of the most quietly important evolutions in Muneeba's interpersonal life.

**Dynamic.** Initially: cool. Not hostile — Muneeba is too disciplined and too principled to be openly hostile to a Muslim woman entering her family — but cool. The published behavioral signature in the early Tyesha scenes is **excessive formal correctness**: Muneeba is impeccably polite, impeccably hospitable, and impeccably *distant*. This is her tell. Warmth, when she withholds it, is withheld in this exact register. The reader who has watched her with Kamala recognizes the difference immediately; Tyesha herself, I assess, registers it within the first meeting.

The cooling is *not* about race in any simple sense, though race is a factor; it is about the broader category Muneeba's first-generation acculturation anxiety attaches to: *the unverified incomer*. Tyesha is unknown. Her family is unknown to the community. Her conversion's depth is, from Muneeba's standpoint, *not yet evidenced*. Muneeba does not trust on declaration; she trusts on demonstration.

**Evolution.** Tyesha demonstrates. Across the Ahmed run and into the late-Wilson and post-Wilson material, Tyesha is depicted as competent, observant, warm, and — importantly — *steady with Aamir*, who is the household's most fragile member in terms of professional and existential drift. As the evidence accumulates, Muneeba's coolness reverses on the same axis as her revisions of judgment about Kamala and Aamir himself: **on evidence, completely, and without retraction**. By the bereavement arcs, Tyesha is functionally inside the household perimeter. She is one of the named figures present at moments of family grief. The transformation is not narrated; it is depicted ambiently, in proximity and posture.

**Trust and safety.** High and rising across the run. Tyesha is, I assess, the figure most likely — if the published timeline extends — to become Muneeba's *successor confidante* as Ruby's generation passes. She has the religious legitimacy, the demonstrated reliability, the inside-the-family position, and — crucially — she is not part of the gossip economy. With Tyesha, Muneeba can speak without monitoring for downstream community leakage.

**Failure mode.** The catastrophic failure scenario is the dissolution of Aamir's marriage. If Tyesha were to leave Aamir, Muneeba's response would be governed by a competition between two principles she usually does not have to choose between: family loyalty (which says: stand with my son) and demonstrated character (which says: Tyesha has not been wrong). Predicted outcome: outward conformity to family loyalty, *private* maintenance of contact with Tyesha through indirect means. Muneeba does not abandon people she has decided to trust.

**Leverage.** Tyesha holds significant leverage by virtue of position: she is the gateway to any grandchildren on the Aamir line, the daily-life caretaker of one of Muneeba's two children, and — post-Kamala — a heightened emotional load-bearing member of the household. Muneeba's counter-leverage is the matriarchal blessing itself, which Tyesha values. The relationship is therefore *mutually invested* and operationally stable.

---

## 4. AAMIR KHAN — *the eldest son, the unexpected ally*

I include Aamir here, despite his being blood, because his function in Muneeba's interpersonal architecture is closer to *ally* than to *child-as-project*. The relational vector with Aamir is different in kind from the one with Kamala.

**Provenance.** Firstborn. The child on whose raising Muneeba presumably made the first-generation mistakes she had corrected by Kamala's adolescence. He emerges in the published record already past the active-discipline phase.

**Dynamic.** Where Kamala drew vigilance, Aamir draws **tolerant exasperation**. His deeper religiosity, his early career drift, his beard, his choice of marriage — these are received by Muneeba in a register of *mild disapproval that does not escalate*. She is observably *less afraid* of him than of Kamala. This is partly gender (her acculturation-anxiety pattern is sharply gendered, as the §3 analysis noted), partly birth order, and partly that Aamir's deviations have always been *toward* tradition rather than away from it — he became more observant than she required, not less. His drift was legible to her in a way Kamala's was not.

**Evolution.** Across the run, Aamir's function evolves from "the older brother who is largely outside the central plot" to "the quietly stabilizing presence in the post-Kamala household." After the bereavement arcs, Aamir is, with Yusuf and Tyesha, one of the three figures who holds the household up while Muneeba metabolizes loss. The depicted dynamic in those scenes is one of **adult son and adult mother**, not parent and dependent — a transition Muneeba accepts more readily with Aamir than the published record suggests she would have with Kamala.

**Trust and safety.** Very high in the practical/logistical/religious domains. Lower in the *confidential affect* domain — Muneeba does not, in published material, bring her deepest griefs to Aamir; she protects him from them, in the same way she protected Kamala from the full weight of Yusuf's cardiac event. The protective instinct does not switch off because the child has grown.

**Failure mode.** Aamir's structural risk to Muneeba is **fragility under sustained adult responsibility**. He is depicted across the run as earnest but somewhat unsteady in worldly matters. If Aamir's life were to collapse — financial failure, marital failure, faith crisis — Muneeba would absorb the cost without complaint and without visible resentment. The failure mode is therefore not relational rupture but *uncompensated burden* on Muneeba herself.

**Leverage.** He holds the leverage of being her last living child. This is a leverage she would not permit him to wield, and that he is constitutionally unlikely to wield, but it is structural. She holds the leverage of being the moral and emotional anchor of the household — a role he depends on more than the published record fully foregrounds.

---

## 5. BRUNO CARRELLI — *the boy across the street; the one she was wrong about*

**Provenance.** Kamala's lifelong friend. White (Italian-American). Non-Muslim. Present in the Khan household, in defiance of Muneeba's stated principles, from the earliest issues, primarily because his presence was negotiated through Kamala's father rather than her mother.

**Dynamic.** Muneeba's depicted posture toward Bruno across the Wilson run is one of **studied non-recognition of his place in Kamala's life**. She is polite. She is feeding him sometimes. She is also, in the early issues, observably maintaining a *fiction* that Bruno is a category of acquaintance rather than the load-bearing emotional figure in her daughter's life that he in fact is. Muneeba is too perceptive (see §3, the Ms. Marvel revelation) not to *know*; the non-recognition is therefore strategic, a way of declining to bless a relationship she does not approve of without escalating to the confrontation that would force the household into open conflict.

**Evolution.** This is the relationship in which Muneeba most clearly **lost** — and accepted that she had lost — a battle of cultural transmission. Bruno is in Kamala's life. Bruno will remain in Kamala's life. Muneeba's evolution is from non-recognition to *grudging operational acceptance* to, after Bruno's various sacrifices on Kamala's behalf in later arcs (including his serious injury), **quiet protective regard**. She never reframes him as a son. But she stops pretending he is not in the family's gravity well. After Kamala's death, his presence in the grief field of the household is, by all available evidence, accepted.

**Trust and safety.** Medium and stable. Muneeba trusts Bruno *with Kamala's safety* — a substantial trust — and does not extend the trust into other domains. She would not consult him. She would not confide. But she would, and I assess did, register that he had been hurt protecting her daughter, and weighted him accordingly thereafter.

**Failure mode.** The historical failure mode — Bruno as the gateway to American cultural drift — has effectively expired by the late run; Kamala's identity is now established and Muneeba has accepted it. The remaining failure mode is more limited: Bruno as a *reminder of Kamala*, intensifying grief in moments Muneeba would prefer containment. The relationship therefore carries a residual ache that has no remediation.

**Leverage.** Bruno holds the leverage of *historical accuracy* — he can correct the Khan family's collective memory of Kamala on points where his recall is more precise than theirs. He has not, to date, exercised this leverage; his deference to the Khans is total. Muneeba holds the leverage of the matriarchal threshold — whether he is welcome in the house. She has, in the late record, kept the threshold open.

---

## 6. THE MASJID WOMEN'S CIRCLE — *the diffuse ally network*

**Provenance.** The women of the Jersey City Masjid — Nakia's mother among them, a rotating cast of aunties whose individual identities are sometimes named and sometimes not. Muneeba is a member of this circle by long-standing participation.

**Dynamic.** This is Muneeba's *infrastructure*. It is the network through which:

- Iftars are coordinated during Ramadan.
- Marriage prospects are quietly surveyed.
- Illness is meal-trained around (the Khans were beneficiaries during Yusuf's cardiac convalescence).
- Bereavement is held collectively after Kamala's death — the women's circle is, in the published material, depicted as performing the practical labor of grief support: food, child-presence, sitting.

Muneeba's role in the circle, I assess from the consistent depiction, is **respected mid-senior**. She is not the matriarch of the circle (that role is held by older women), but she is one of its trusted operators. She is the kind of member whose opinion on a contested matter is sought.

**Evolution.** Stable across the run. The circle pre-dates the published record and post-dates Kamala's death. It is the most *durable* of all Muneeba's social structures and the one least dependent on any single individual.

**Trust and safety.** Domain-specific. The circle is trusted with practical labor and ritual support, *not* with secrets. Information shared with the circle is information shared with the community.

**Failure mode.** Schism. Religious-community circles of this kind are vulnerable to factional rupture over doctrinal, ethnic, or interpersonal disputes. If the circle fractured, Muneeba would lose her largest practical support network. Her assessed response: alignment with the faction containing the older matriarchs, whose authority she respects, even at the cost of friendships with peer-members.

**Leverage.** The circle's collective leverage over Muneeba is the same as Ruby's individual leverage, scaled up: it can elevate or damage the Khan family's standing. Muneeba's counter-leverage is her own demonstrated reliability — she is a *contributor* to the circle's labor, not merely a beneficiary, and this banked credit is substantial.

---

## 7. NAKIA BAHADIR — *the daughter's friend, the inherited niece*

**Provenance.** Kamala's closest female friend. Turkish-American, observant Muslim, hijabi. Present in the Khan household from Kamala's earliest issues, and — critically for Muneeba's classification of her — *pre-approved by category*: a hijabi Muslim girl from a known community family.

**Dynamic.** Of all Kamala's friends, Nakia is the one Muneeba **categorically approves of without reservation**. Nakia's presence does not require the studied non-recognition that Bruno's does; she is welcomed openly, fed warmly, addressed in the affectionate diminutives Muneeba reserves for inside-the-perimeter young people. The dynamic is essentially that of an honorary niece.

**Evolution.** Across the run, Nakia is depicted with increasing closeness to the Khan household, and post-Kamala she is one of the figures whose continued presence in Muneeba's life is, I assess, *load-bearing*. She is a living connection to Kamala that does not carry Bruno's complicated valence — Nakia and Kamala's friendship was framed in the moral-cultural register Muneeba can fully metabolize.

**Trust and safety.** High and uncomplicated. The simplest relationship on this list. There is no operational complexity; Nakia is *categorically inside* and has done nothing to displace that classification.

**Failure mode.** The most plausible failure mode is **over-reliance** — Muneeba leaning on Nakia, post-bereavement, in ways that ask Nakia to occupy a daughter-shaped space she did not consent to occupy. The published record does not yet show this, but it is a structural risk of the relationship's deepening.

**Leverage.** Nakia holds significant *emotional* leverage post-bereavement: her presence comforts, her absence would wound. She does not, by character, exercise leverage. Muneeba holds the leverage of being a maternal-elder figure to Nakia in Nakia's own life — a role that is itself a gift Muneeba is, post-Kamala, in a position to give.

---

## SYNTHESIS — THE TOPOLOGY OF MUNEEBA'S CHOSEN FIELD

Mapped together, the relational field has a recognizable structure:

**An inner ring** — Yusuf (covered in Relationships I), Aamir, Tyesha, Nakia. High trust, daily-life proximity, affect-permitted. Four figures.

**A middle ring** — Auntie Ruby, Bruno. Medium trust, asymmetric, compartmentalized. Each holds a specific kind of access and a specific kind of risk.

**An institutional ring** — Sheikh Abdullah, the masjid women's circle. Domain-specific trust, formal, durable, role-bound rather than person-bound.

The architecture is **resilient by design** — no single rupture collapses the field. It is also **narrow by design** — the inner ring is small enough that the loss of any one member (as with Kamala) is catastrophic and uncompensable. Muneeba's containment strategy works at every level except the level of the irreplaceable individual, and at that level it does not work at all; it merely holds the surrounding architecture upright while she endures what cannot be contained.

This is the file's most important finding about her chosen relationships: she does not build redundancy where redundancy is impossible. She loves the specific people, accepts the specific risks, and trusts her containment to hold the rest of the world steady while the unsurvivable is, nevertheless, survived.

*End section. Relationships III (Adversaries, Antagonists, Strained Ties) to follow.*


## Relationships III — Rivals, Enemies & Lovers

# RELATIONSHIPS III — RIVALS, ENEMIES & LOVERS

*Sub-dossier scope note: The subject's life, as published, is structurally devoid of "enemies" in the operational sense — no antagonists hunt her, no rivals contest her domain in the workplace or political register, no lovers exist outside her marriage. This is itself a finding. A woman of her age, community standing, and visibility within a tightly observed diaspora congregation in Jersey City would, under total surveillance, generate a thicker rival/enemy ledger than the canonical record supplies. What the file therefore documents is the **functional analogues**: the social rivals of the masjid auntie-circuit, the cultural antagonists she has named in her own speech, the singular intimate partner of her adult life, and the structural enemies — entities, not persons — that have actually cost her something. Each is mapped to the same depth as a named adversary would be in a conventional dossier.*

---

## I. RIVALS

### I.a — "Auntie Ruby" (Rubina Aunty)

The most consistently named figure in Muneeba's social ecosystem outside her household. Across the Wilson run she is invoked roughly a dozen times, almost always as a threat-vector ("what will Auntie Ruby say?"), occasionally as a confidant, never as a peer-equal. The relationship is not friendship in the Western sense; it is the *primary node* of Muneeba's reputational network.

**History.** Auntie Ruby predates Kamala in the household lexicon — she is established mythology by *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #1, requiring no introduction. The two women are co-members of the Circle Q–adjacent ISNJ-style masjid community, almost certainly arrived in Jersey City within a few years of each other in the late 1980s–early 1990s immigrant wave, raised children in parallel, and have spent two decades on the same Eid catering rotations, condolence visits, and wedding-prep committees. They are not blood; the "auntie" honorific is community-relational.

**Dynamic.** Muneeba's relationship to Ruby is the textbook diaspora-cohort *frenemy* configuration: mutual surveillance dressed as mutual concern. Each woman is the other's reputational mirror. Information flows both ways with calibrated leakage — Muneeba shares what she wants the community to know, withholds what she does not, and is fully aware Ruby is doing the same. Neither is naïve.

The asymmetry: Ruby is the network's *amplifier*, Muneeba is the network's *judge*. Ruby has the wider gossip surface; Muneeba has the higher moral standing. Ruby therefore needs Muneeba's tacit endorsement to validate the gossip she circulates; Muneeba needs Ruby's circulation to enforce community norms without personally appearing to do so. This is a functional partnership that both women would describe as friendship and a UATU-grade reader would describe as a stable, low-intensity status pact.

**Evolution.** Cooler in the Wilson early issues (Ruby weaponized against Kamala as a disciplinary specter); warmer and more intimate during the Yusuf cardiac arc, where Ruby almost certainly delivered food and sat with Muneeba; cooler again, in the inferential post-Kamala's-death period, because Ruby's role as community amplifier becomes intolerable when *one's own grief* is the broadcast subject. The bereavement era likely produced the most significant strain in their relationship the file contains, though it is depicted only obliquely.

**Trust / Safety.** Mid-tier. Muneeba does not confide deep emotion to Ruby. She confides logistical complaints (a son's marriage, a husband's diet) which Ruby reliably transmits with Muneeba's preferred framing. She would not tell Ruby about her foreknowledge of Kamala's heroism; she did not even tell Yusuf for some time.

**Failure mode.** A breach of the implicit pact — Ruby circulating something Muneeba had marked private, or rendering Muneeba herself as gossip-subject rather than gossip-co-author. The probable response is not confrontation; it is a slow, polite, structurally devastating withdrawal of presence at the women's gatherings Ruby chairs, which the community would read instantly.

**Leverage.** Ruby's primary leverage over Muneeba is the threat of social narration — the power to render any household event in a frame Muneeba did not choose. Muneeba's leverage over Ruby is moral standing: a single cool sentence from Muneeba about Ruby's conduct would shift the masjid women's room.

---

### I.b — The Generalized Auntie-Circuit (Composite Rival)

Beyond Ruby, the file infers a standing roster of perhaps six to ten women — masjid regulars, mothers of Aamir's and Kamala's peers, neighbors — who function as a collective rival. They are not enemies. They are *the gallery*. Muneeba's life is performed in part for their evaluation, and she performs for theirs, and each woman is keenly aware that her children's marriage prospects, her husband's professional referrals, and her own old-age care will be mediated through this network's verdict.

**Dynamic.** Comparative. The currency is children's accomplishments, husbands' health, the visible cleanliness of one's home during unannounced visits, the quality of one's cooking at communal meals, and — most acutely — the perceived religiosity and modesty of one's daughters. Muneeba is *competitive* in this register in a way she would not name as competition. Her insistence on Kamala's clothing, her early disapproval of Bruno-as-friend, her firmness about curfews — all are partially driven by anticipatory defense of her ranking in this gallery.

**Trust / Safety.** Low individually, moderate collectively. The gallery as a whole is *safe* in the sense that Muneeba knows its rules cold; individual members are tactical actors whose specific moves she tracks.

**Failure mode.** A daughter visibly out of pocket — caught at a party, dressed wrong at a public event, dating outside the faith — registers in this network as a *maternal failure*, and the file confirms (via Kamala's repeated invocation of her mother's anticipated reaction) that this is the discipline-pressure Muneeba most reliably internalizes and transmits.

**Leverage.** This network is the single most effective lever any actor could pull on Muneeba, and Kamala intuits it as a child intuits the path through a forest. The auntie-circuit's collective verdict is also what makes her acceptance of Tyesha — a Black American convert — a *significant* moral act and not a small one. Muneeba had to be willing to be re-ranked by the gallery to do it, and the canonical evidence is that she was.

---

### I.c — Zoe Zimmer (early-era proxy rival)

Not a rival in any direct sense — Muneeba and Zoe almost certainly have never spoken. But Zoe is the *embodied form* of what Muneeba is rivaling: the blonde, affluent, religiously unmarked American girl whose social ease Kamala envies and whose lifestyle Muneeba reads as a category of risk. In the early issues Muneeba's prohibitions track Zoe-adjacent activities (parties, mixed gatherings, late nights) with surgical precision. Muneeba is *rivaling Zoe for Kamala's identity*, and she knows it.

**Evolution.** This rivalry dissolves as Kamala's social world matures, as Zoe herself proves more complex than the early framing, and as Muneeba's own anxieties about cultural transmission relax post-Ms.-Marvel-reveal. By the late Wilson run this rival-vector is functionally retired.

**Leverage / Failure mode.** Inapplicable — Zoe never knew she was a competitor, and Muneeba never named her one aloud.

---

## II. ENEMIES

The published canon supplies no named human enemy of Muneeba Khan. The dossier therefore maps the **structural antagonists** — the forces that have actually inflicted cost on her — at the depth a named enemy would receive.

### II.a — Catastrophe-Class Threats to Kamala (the unfaceable enemy)

The Inventor, Kamran, Bruno's accidents, Discord, the assorted villains of the Wilson and Ahmed runs, and ultimately whichever entity ended Kamala's life in the *Amazing Spider-Man*–adjacent material — these are, from Muneeba's vantage, a single composite enemy: *the thing that hunts my daughter*. Muneeba does not know most of their names. She knows their effects: missed curfews, exhaustion, bruises explained as gym mishaps, eventually a closed casket.

**Dynamic.** The enemy is undefeatable on Muneeba's terms because she cannot meet it on its plane. Her response — strict curfews, then, post-reveal, scaffolded normalcy and prayer — is the only response available to a parent who has accepted that her child operates in a domain her competence cannot reach. The acceptance is itself the file's most quietly devastating data point.

**Failure mode.** Realized. Kamala died.

**Leverage.** The enemy has none over Muneeba directly because there is no further demand it can make; it took the maximum and she absorbed it without decompensating. This is the single strongest evidence in the entire file for the resilience profile asserted in §3.

---

### II.b — The State (as latent antagonist)

A first-generation Pakistani-American Muslim woman in post-2001 Jersey City lives, by demographic position, in a low-grade adversarial relationship with several state and quasi-state apparatuses: TSA, immigration enforcement adjacencies, NYPD intelligence (the documented Demographics Unit surveilled exactly her community in exactly her period), school administrators, and — in the Marvel universe — Damage Control, S.H.I.E.L.D. successors, and any post-*Civil War II* registration-adjacent apparatus.

The canonical evidence for Muneeba's awareness of this is indirect but consistent: her insistence on documentation, her careful dress in public-official contexts, her counsel to her children about *how to be seen*. She is not depicted as politicized in the activist register, but she is depicted as *operationally cautious* in the manner of a person who has correctly assessed her household's standing with respect to state attention.

**Dynamic.** Defensive, not confrontational. Muneeba's strategy is invisibility-through-respectability: be so obviously law-abiding, so obviously a contributing family, that the state's interest does not alight. This strategy is partially effective, partially humiliating, and entirely unreciprocated by the state in any documented way.

**Failure mode.** Any incident that breaks the invisibility — a son detained, a daughter publicly named in a super-incident, a husband's hospital admission generating bureaucratic exposure. The Ms. Marvel public-reveal arcs put extraordinary strain on exactly this strategy, and Muneeba's quiet management of it is one of the file's underappreciated competencies.

**Leverage.** The state has structural leverage over the family it has not, in canon, chosen to deploy. Muneeba has none in return.

---

### II.c — Time / Acculturation Drift

Not a person, but the antagonist Muneeba names most often in her own voice. Her grip on her daughter's clothing, food, friends, prayer schedule, and language is a daily skirmish with the slow enemy of *Americanization-as-erosion*. The enemy advances regardless of her tactics; she loses ground every year, and she knows it.

**Dynamic.** Asymmetric attrition. Muneeba cannot win this engagement; she can only set the rate of loss. Her post-reveal pivot with Kamala is, in part, recognition that the original strategy (high friction, high prohibition) was producing accelerated loss and that *trust extended* slows attrition better than *trust withheld*.

**Failure mode.** Realized intermittently across Kamala's adolescence; mitigated, not eliminated, by Muneeba's mid-course correction.

**Leverage.** None available. The relationship to this enemy is the closest Muneeba comes, in the file, to a stance of *acceptance without surrender* — a religiously inflected stoicism that does the daily work without expecting victory.

---

### II.d — Yusuf's Heart (the intimate enemy)

The cardiac condition is mapped here, not in the medical section, because in the operational register of Muneeba's life it functions as an *adversary* — an entity that threatens to take her partner, that requires daily counter-measures (medication, diet, stress management), that cannot be defeated and can only be held off. Muneeba has been engaged with this enemy for years.

**Dynamic.** Vigilant, quiet, unrelenting. She manages Yusuf's pillbox, his salt intake, his exposure to family stressors. She does not tell Kamala the full picture. She does not tell Ruby. She absorbs the cognitive load alone, which is consistent with her containment profile and is also, on the evidence, what she prefers.

**Failure mode.** A second cardiac event, particularly post-Kamala's death, would be the most plausible breach point in Muneeba's containment system. The file does not depict this. If it occurred, the §3 prediction is that her religious-practice scaffold and role-based identity would hold, but the margin would be thinner than it has been to date.

**Leverage.** This enemy has the most leverage over Muneeba of any entity in her file, because Yusuf is the relationship her self-organization depends on most directly. See §III.

---

## III. INTIMATES / LOVERS

### III.a — Yusuf Khan (Husband; sole intimate partner of record)

The only romantic and sexual partner in Muneeba's published life. The marriage is depicted across all eras of the Wilson and Ahmed runs as functional, affectionate, equitable, and — most diagnostically — *companionate in the deep sense*. They negotiate. They tease. They disagree about the children, sometimes pointedly, and resolve the disagreement without rupture.

**History.** The marriage is established as predating the family's arrival in the United States or as having been formed in the immigration-era hardship period obliquely referenced in canon. Aamir is the elder child by several years; Kamala arrived later. The marital arc is therefore on the order of three decades by the time of the early Wilson issues, and four by the bereavement era. They have weathered immigration, child-rearing, a major cardiac event, the discovery of a daughter's secret superhero identity, and the daughter's death. The marriage has not, in canonical evidence, fractured under any of this.

**Dynamic.** Yusuf is the warmer, more openly affectionate partner in the public/domestic register; Muneeba is the operational center. He provides her the *permission to be tender* that she does not extend herself easily — when Yusuf is sentimental at the dinner table, Muneeba's eye-roll is the cover that lets her smile. He is, in the precise behavioral sense, her *affect-extender*: she experiences a broader emotional range in his presence than she displays in any other relationship documented in the file.

The division of labor in their marriage tracks gendered conventions of their cohort but is not rigid. Yusuf is the breadwinner of record; Muneeba runs the household economy, the religious calendar, the children's developmental tracking, and — post-cardiac-event — the family's medical management and a non-trivial share of its administrative load. Decisions about the children are joint, with Muneeba carrying greater weight on Kamala-specific matters and Yusuf often weighing in as the softer voice.

**Evolution.** Era One (pre-canon through early Wilson): conventional, durable, lightly affectionate in public. Era Two (Yusuf's illness): a deepening — Muneeba's competence shifts into a protective mode toward Yusuf that mirrors her protection of the children. Era Three (post-Ms.-Marvel-reveal): Muneeba carries the secret first; the eventual sharing of it with Yusuf is one of the unwritten but inferable marital scenes of the run. Era Four (post-Kamala's death): the marriage is the load-bearing wall. Both partners are bereaved; neither collapses; each almost certainly carries the other in alternating shifts in a way the published material gestures at without fully depicting.

**Trust / Safety.** Highest available in the file. Muneeba's containment relaxes more in Yusuf's presence than anywhere else documented. She speaks more, jokes more (her dry register, referenced in §3, is largely visible only when Yusuf is the audience), shows physical tenderness more readily. The bedroom — depicted only by implication, as is appropriate to the property — is the room in which Muneeba is most fully herself.

**Intimacy register.** Their canonical physical affection is modest in display (a hand on a shoulder, a forehead kiss, brief embraces) but consistent and unforced. The intimacy reads as long-married rather than new — comfortable contact without performance. There is no canonical evidence of marital infidelity by either party, no evidence of considered separation, no evidence of sustained estrangement. The marriage is, by the available record, monogamous, stable, and warm.

**Failure modes.** Three identifiable risk vectors:
1. *Yusuf's death*. The single largest unrealized stressor in Muneeba's file. Her containment system has absorbed a daughter's death; whether it would absorb a husband's is the open empirical question of her psychology, and the §3 estimate (it would hold, with narrowing margin) is the best available read but is not certain.
2. *A second secret of comparable magnitude to Kamala's heroism*, held by Yusuf and disclosed late. There is no evidence such a secret exists. If it did, Muneeba's response would draw on the same evidence-updating capacity that absorbed the Ms. Marvel reveal — but the betrayal-vector inherent to a *partner's* concealment, rather than a child's, would cut differently.
3. *Cumulative caregiving load* in a long widowhood-precursor period — a sustained decline in Yusuf's health that requires Muneeba to be the indefinite primary caregiver while she is herself unsupported. This is the slow-failure scenario.

**Leverage.** Yusuf has more leverage over Muneeba than any other person living or dead, including Kamala, because Yusuf is the relationship from which Muneeba draws the permission to be the broader self the rest of her life keeps contained. Any actor who understood Muneeba's psychology would identify Yusuf as the load-bearing intimate and act accordingly. He himself, on the evidence, deploys this leverage almost never — when he does, it is to soften her toward the children, and she nearly always yields.

---

### III.b — Absence of any other lover, past or present

The dossier records this as a positive finding rather than a gap. No prior engagements, no pre-marital romantic history, no extramarital interest, no widowed-period entanglement (Yusuf remains living in the available canon), no emotionally-intimate non-sexual male relationships outside the family. Muneeba's romantic file is a single, decades-long, monogamous entry.

This is consistent with — but not reducible to — the cultural and religious frame she operates within. It is also consistent with her broader psychological profile: a person organized around containment, role-fidelity, and durable commitment does not generate a wide romantic ledger, and Muneeba does not.

**Operational implication.** A subject with one intimate partner of record has one intimate-partner vulnerability of record. The entire weight of her romantic-attachment system rests on Yusuf. This concentrates risk, but it also concentrates resilience: the marriage is the asset, not a portfolio of relationships, and the asset has, to date, performed.

---

*End sub-section. Cross-reference §III (Psychological), §V (Personality — interpersonal pattern, pressure points), and the forthcoming Relationships II (Family) for full mapping of the Yusuf relationship's intersections with the parental dyad and the bereavement arc.*


## Powers, Abilities & Their Limits

# POWERS, ABILITIES & THEIR LIMITS — SUBJECT: MUNEEBA KHAN

*Stage-Two Capability Mapping. The subject is a civilian. This section therefore catalogues her competencies — domestic, social, perceptual, moral — as a total-surveillance file would catalogue an operative's tradecraft, because in functional terms that is what they are. Muneeba Khan exercises power; the power is just legibly maternal rather than superhuman.*

---

## 1. THE CORE CAPABILITY: HOUSEHOLD COMMAND

The single most consistent depiction across a decade of canon is that Muneeba runs the Khan household as its operational center. Yusuf is its titular and spiritual head; Muneeba is its logistics, intelligence, finance, and discipline directorate. The split is visible from *Ms. Marvel* (2014) #1 onward: when a permission, a meal, a curfew, a school issue, a wedding cost, or a medication refill is at stake, the question routes to her, not to him, and her ruling is final unless Yusuf is specifically consulted on a religious-jurisprudential point.

**Mechanism.** She holds the household's full state in working memory: who is where, who has eaten, who owes what, who has prayed, who is angry with whom, what is in the freezer, when Aamir last called, what Auntie Ruby last said. This is not depicted as effortful; it is depicted as ambient. She corrects Kamala's account of a small fact (a time, a place, a friend's surname) reflexively, in passing, while doing something else with her hands. Total-surveillance reading: the subject maintains a continuously updated mental ledger of approximately fifteen to twenty active interpersonal threads and approximately fifty to eighty recurring logistical variables, and queries it in milliseconds.

**Range.** The nuclear household; the extended Khan/Jan kin network on two continents (visible in the wedding arc and in periodic phone calls to Karachi referenced obliquely); the Jersey City masjid circle; the immediate neighbors; the school-parent perimeter. She is *not* operationally fluent outside these rings — she does not navigate the white professional-class Jersey City world her daughter slips between, and she does not attempt to.

**Limits.** Granularity collapses outside her perimeter. She cannot model what Kamala is doing in Avengers Tower, with Bruno after midnight, or in the costume; her early-era monitoring failures are not failures of vigilance but of *jurisdictional reach*. The Ms. Marvel reveal moment (#19) is partly Muneeba acknowledging this limit: she watched as far as she could, inferred the rest, and chose not to interrogate the unobservable.

---

## 2. PERCEPTUAL ABILITIES — THE QUIET INSTRUMENT

The most underestimated capability in her file is her perceptual acuity. She is, functionally, the household's intelligence analyst.

**Signal collection.** She reads micro-changes: a shift in Kamala's appetite, a new lock on a door, a phone turned face-down, a story whose details migrate between tellings, a smell on a coat (smoke, ozone, the city), a missing earring, a new bruise pattern incompatible with the claimed cause. Across the Wilson run she is shown noticing each of these and *not naming what she has noticed* — a deliberate withholding that distinguishes her from the stereotype of the interrogating immigrant mother she superficially resembles.

**Signature deduction — the Ms. Marvel inference.** She arrives at the correct identification of her daughter as Ms. Marvel without disclosure, without confession, and without confrontation. This is the file's central demonstration of her perceptual ceiling. The inference required integrating: physical evidence (torn clothing, exhaustion patterns, schedule anomalies), correlation of Kamala's absences with public Ms. Marvel sightings, behavioral evidence (Kamala's reactions to news coverage, to the name "Ms. Marvel" said in the room), and a willingness to entertain a hypothesis her cultural-religious priors would normally exclude. She did all of this silently, over months, and then *sat on the conclusion*. This is not maternal intuition. This is intelligence work.

**Limits.** Her perceptual range is keenest within the household and degrades with distance. She misreads Bruno persistently (overestimating romantic threat, underestimating loyalty) because Bruno occupies a category — non-Muslim boy adjacent to her daughter — her schema processes by category rather than by individual. She underread Aamir's spiritual seriousness for years before updating. Her instrument is sharp but its calibration is culturally weighted; novel categories trigger schema-based shortcuts before individuated observation.

**Symptom-as-signature.** When Muneeba *stops asking questions* about a domain, it does not mean she has lost interest; it means she has reached a conclusion and is choosing the timing of its disclosure. The silence is the tell.

---

## 3. AFFECT-REGULATION ABILITIES — THE CONTAINMENT FACULTY

Muneeba's capacity to compress and time-shift her own emotional expression is, in the operational sense, a *power*. It is the faculty that allows her to function as the household's stabilizing mass.

**Mechanism.** She separates the experience of affect from its expression by a deliberate lag, usually filled with a physical task — wiping a counter, adjusting a dupatta, pouring tea, beginning a prayer. The task absorbs the somatic charge; the expression, when it arrives, is calibrated. This is visible in the cardiac-event arc with Yusuf: she receives news of his condition, completes the immediate logistical sequence (hospital, calls, medication schedule), and only afterwards, in private, allows the affect through. Kamala witnesses only the calibrated layer.

**Range and ceiling.** The faculty holds through her husband's cardiac crisis, through the Incursion (where it deliberately dissolves under conditions she has selected), through Aamir's marriage stress, and — most strikingly — through her daughter's death. The *Fallen Friend* and *Death of* material depict her grief as nearly mute in the public-facing register, with the affect routed into religious practice and household provisioning rather than into demonstration.

**Limits.** The faculty is not unbounded. It is shown to dissolve voluntarily under two conditions: (1) catastrophic threat to a child, when the disciplinary register is dropped in favor of open physical tenderness (the *Last Days* embrace); (2) genuine private intimacy with Yusuf, where partnered affection is depicted as easy and unguarded. There is also an *involuntary* dissolution threshold the file has not yet tested — the death of Yusuf would be the unsurveilled experiment. Based on pattern extrapolation, the prediction is not decompensation but a deepening of the same containment to near-silence.

**Symptom-as-signature.** When her speech *shortens* and her hands *find a task*, she is at high affective load. When she becomes verbally elaborate or scriptural, the load is moderate and she is processing. When she is openly tender, the load has either exceeded the containment ceiling or she has chosen to release it.

---

## 4. DISCIPLINARY TRADECRAFT — THE WITHDRAWAL TOOLKIT

Muneeba's disciplinary toolkit is narrow, refined, and almost never escalates to volume.

**Tier one — the look.** A single sustained gaze, sometimes accompanied by Kamala's full name. Effective on minor infractions. Range: line of sight, household perimeter.

**Tier two — cold register.** Voice flattens, address shifts from affectionate diminutives ("*beta*", "*jaan*") to neutral or formal forms. Conversation continues but emotional warmth is withdrawn. This is her workhorse tool through the early issues and is psychologically expensive for Kamala precisely because it is non-violent and non-loud — there is nothing to push back against.

**Tier three — exclusion from confidence.** Information stops flowing toward the offender. Plans are made without consultation. This is the rarest and most punishing tier and is reserved for serious moral matters.

**Tier four — direct confrontation.** Used perhaps three or four times in published canon. Always seated, always one-on-one, always with the door closed. Distinguishable from lower tiers by her use of explicitly moral-religious vocabulary.

**What is conspicuously absent:** corporal discipline, screaming, threats of expulsion from the family, ultimatums she could not enforce, weaponized comparison to other children inside the household. Her use of community comparison ("what will Auntie Ruby say?") is a lever but a *bounded* one; she does not deploy it to humiliate, only to indicate the cost surface of a behavior.

**Growth over time.** Through the Wilson run she relies on tiers one and two heavily, tier three occasionally. Post-revelation (#19 onward) the toolkit shrinks: she retains tier one for minor matters (driving, grades), almost retires tier two, and replaces tier three with explicit consultative conversation. The toolkit's atrophy is a measure of trust extended.

---

## 5. RELIGIOUS-RITUAL COMPETENCE

She is observant at a level functionally equivalent to a working lay scholar of household practice — not a *hafiza*, not a credentialed teacher, but fluent in the daily fiqh of cooking, dress, prayer timing, holiday observance, hospitality, and the social-religious obligations of a community elder-in-training.

**Specific competencies depicted or strongly implied:** halal kitchen management at scale (she cooks for guests routinely and at religious occasions in volume); Ramadan logistics for a household with varying ages and a cardiac patient; Eid coordination across the extended kin network; janazah and mourning protocols (deployed during the bereavement arc); wedding-rite coordination (visible in the Aamir-Tyesha arc); hijab/dress protocol management for herself and contextually for Kamala.

**The ritual faculty as integrative tool.** Religious practice functions for her as the primary integrator of affect, time, and meaning. Prayer is not depicted as performative or as ego-syntonic ritualism; it is depicted as the place she goes when affect must be processed. After the cardiac event, after the Incursion, after the death — the camera, when granted private access, finds her at prayer or immediately adjacent to it.

**Limits.** She is not theologically combative; she does not debate doctrine, does not contest interpretations, does not engage with the more contested *jurisprudential* questions that more scholastically inclined characters in the same canon (Aamir, certain mosque figures) take up. Her religion is *practiced* more than *argued*. This is a strength, not a weakness — it is what makes the faculty integrative rather than divisive.

---

## 6. SOCIAL-DIPLOMATIC ABILITIES

Within her three primary social rings (kin, masjid, neighborhood), Muneeba operates with high diplomatic competence.

**Reputation management.** She maintains the family's standing through a long-running, low-cost campaign of visible respectability: appropriate dress, regular attendance, contribution to community functions, careful management of which family difficulties are visible and which are not. Yusuf's cardiac event is *visible* (a matter for community prayer); Kamala's costumed life is *invisible* (a matter for the household alone). The line between visible and invisible is drawn by Muneeba and is consistent.

**Coalition behavior.** She maintains a working alliance with Auntie Ruby and the masjid women that gives her early access to community information and a buffer of social capital. She has not, in the published record, been the subject of community gossip; she has been a node *through which* community information flows.

**The Tyesha negotiation.** Her handling of Aamir's choice of a Black American convert as his wife is a master-class diplomatic sequence: initial visible coolness (signaling to community that traditional preferences were not casually abandoned), private investigation of Tyesha's character and sincerity, gradual public warmth (signaling endorsement once warranted), and post-marriage full integration of Tyesha into the kin network. The arc is paced over months and is executed without any single confrontational moment.

**Limits.** Outside the three rings, she does not operate. She is not depicted negotiating with school administrators, with employers, with civic institutions; that domain is handled by Yusuf, by Aamir as he ages into it, or by Kamala. Her diplomatic faculty is *intra-community* and does not generalize to American institutional space.

---

## 7. GROWTH ARC OF THE CAPABILITIES

Across the published decade, the capabilities do not *expand* so much as they *redistribute*.

- The perceptual faculty was always at ceiling; what changed is her willingness to *act on what she perceived* by speaking it aloud (the Ms. Marvel disclosure, the Tyesha embrace, the Aamir endorsement).
- The disciplinary toolkit shrank as trust extended, with tier two largely retired post-#19.
- The containment faculty deepened under successive losses without breaking.
- The religious-ritual faculty was load-tested by bereavement and held.
- The social-diplomatic faculty matured into something closer to community-elder posture in the later issues.

The trajectory is not the *acquisition* of new abilities but the *consolidation* of existing ones into a more integrated, less defended whole. By the post-resurrection material she is operating at fewer tiers and with less concealment than she did in 2014, and her household is more functional, not less, for it.

---

## 8. SIGNATURE APPLICATIONS

Three sequences in canon constitute the signature applications of her composite capability set.

**The Incursion embrace (*Ms. Marvel* #16–19, *Last Days*).** Under the perceived end of the world, every capability is deployed simultaneously and in correct order: containment is *deliberately released*, the perceptual faculty reads Kamala's terror correctly, ritual practice (prayer together) integrates the moment, and the disciplinary toolkit is set aside entirely. The sequence demonstrates that the strictness was a *role*, not a personality.

**The Ms. Marvel disclosure (#19).** Months of silent perceptual work, a containment hold across that entire interval, a single calibrated release of the held conclusion, and the explicit transfer of the relationship onto consultative footing. The cleanest single demonstration of her tradecraft.

**The bereavement arc.** Containment, ritual, and household provisioning sustain her and the family through the death of her daughter without depicted decompensation. The capability set is here load-tested at the ceiling and holds.

---

## 9. THE SYMPTOM-AS-SIGNATURE READING

The faculties resolve into a single signature: **Muneeba Khan converts what would, in a less integrated subject, present as symptoms — hypervigilance, suppression, control, religiosity, social conservatism — into instruments.** The hypervigilance is intelligence collection. The suppression is timed disclosure. The control is household command. The religiosity is affective integration. The social conservatism is reputation management.
