**Mechanism 2 — Provision to a child who needs her.** When Kamala or Aamir presents an actual need — not a manufactured one, which she sees through — Muneeba's distress reorganizes around the provision. This is the mechanism most reliably exploitable by an observer wishing to bring her out of a withdrawn state, and it is the mechanism Kamala intuitively reached for during the *Last Days* arc.

**Mechanism 3 — Sajdah.** The position of prostration in salah appears, across the run, as her single most reliable affect-regulation tool. She is shown in sajdah longer than the prayer requires at the most stressed moments of the canonical record. Whatever the theological content of that position for her, its behavioral function is regulatory. A surveillance file would log prayer duration as a continuous variable; Muneeba's prayer length is her clearest interior indicator.

---

## 6.6 SUMMARY FINDING

Muneeba Khan's failure profile is unusually well-defended for her demographic and history. The container holds because it is multiply-redundant: religious practice, role identity, marital partnership, household competence, and community standing each provide independent structural support, and the failure of any one is absorbed by the others. The decompensation, when it has occurred in canon, has been *grief without symptom*, *loss without collapse*, *injury without rupture* — and this is not denial but a genuine integrative achievement, the product of a life organized around the practice of containment as a moral discipline rather than as a defense against unbearable affect.

The conditions that could produce true collapse exist, are enumerable, and are largely untested in published material. The single most dangerous of them — accusation by Kamala that the early strictness caused harm — sits within the family's reach at all times and has, by tacit mutual agreement, never been activated. That this lever has not been pulled is itself a datum: the daughter has read the mother more accurately than the early issues credited her with, and has elected to leave the container intact.

The dossier's final operational note: **the absence of dry humor is the alarm.** Everything else can be misread. That cannot.

*End §6. Continue to §7: Operational Profile & Network Map.*


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT — MUNEEBA KHAN

*Classification: Stage-Two Predictive Dossier. Projections derive from longitudinal behavioral patterns documented in the Stage-One workup; confidence intervals noted where the evidence base is thin.*

---

## 6.1 BASELINE TRAJECTORY VECTOR

The defining fact about Muneeba Khan's forward trajectory is that she is, at the published terminus of her record, a woman whose central organizing function — the daily monitoring and moral scaffolding of an adolescent daughter — has been twice disrupted: first by the Ms. Marvel revelation (which structurally promoted Kamala from supervised minor to acknowledged adult-with-mission), and second by Kamala's death and resurrection-as-mutant (which permanently altered the legibility of the daughter she thought she had finished raising).

A subject organized around *containment* requires *something to contain*. With Kamala materially beyond her capacity to protect — superhuman, mutant, networked into the X-Men's logistical apparatus, no longer in the household, no longer of the same ontological category as her parents — Muneeba enters middle age (early-to-mid fifties by best estimate from the Wilson timeline; the published record is deliberately imprecise) with a contracting container and an undiminished capacity. This is the structural pressure that will shape the next decade of her life regardless of what particular plots are written around her.

The baseline forward vector, absent disruption, is therefore a **redistribution of containment energy** toward the available substrates: Yusuf's failing health, Aamir and Tyesha's marriage and any forthcoming grandchildren, the Jersey City masjid community, and — the wildcard — her own interior life, which the canonical record has never required her to inhabit alone.

---

## 6.2 LIKELY DEVELOPMENTS, ENUMERATED

**Within 12–24 months (high confidence):**

She will become the primary medical advocate for Yusuf. The cardiac event of the Ahmed run is not a one-time plot device but a chronic condition; she will be the one calling cardiology, refilling prescriptions, learning the Medicare-supplement paperwork, modifying the dinner menu, and absorbing — without disclosure to her children — the running probability calculation about how long he has. Expect her phone to acquire pill-reminder alarms she did not set herself (Aamir will have installed them); expect her to override them and run her own mnemonic system, because she does not delegate the things that matter.

She will inherit a more visible role at the masjid — committee work, the women's halaqa, organizing the Eid logistics — partly because grief makes such work consoling and partly because the community will *give* it to her as a recognized form of honoring Kamala. She will accept it with the same restrained competence she brings to everything; she will not, however, become a public figure of her grief. There will be a specific photograph of Kamala she keeps in her wallet that she will never show anyone, including Yusuf, who has his own.

She will visit Kamala — wherever Kamala physically lives post-resurrection — on a schedule she sets and enforces. The visits will be structurally ritualized (food brought, specific dishes Kamala requested as a child, no overnight stays at first), and Muneeba will not ask the questions she most wants to ask. The non-asking is itself the management strategy.

**Within 3–5 years (moderate confidence):**

Tyesha and Aamir will have at least one child, and Muneeba will become a grandmother. This is the single most predictable transformation in her file. The grandmother register will be markedly different from the mother register: looser on rules, freer with physical affection, openly sentimental in a way she never permitted herself with her own children. Grandparenthood will function as a redemptive second pass at the parts of mothering her early-era control style foreclosed. She will notice this. She will not name it.

The relationship with Tyesha will deepen into something like the friendship Muneeba never had with her own mother (inferable from the published immigration backstory's silences). Tyesha is a convert; Muneeba will become, in time, her mother-in-Islam as well as her mother-in-law, and this will be one of the quiet honors of her later life. Expect a recurring weekly visit, a specific shared task (Quran study, recipe documentation, the slow translation of Muneeba's mother's recipes from intuition into written measurement for the grandchildren).

Her relationship with Kamala will renegotiate around the mutant identity. This is the harder projection. Muneeba has demonstrated capacity to update on evidence; she has not been required to update on *category*. A mutant daughter, in the current Marvel sociopolitical environment, is not the same management problem as a superhero daughter. There is anti-mutant prejudice in her own community to be navigated; there is the question of whether her grandchildren-by-Aamir might also manifest; there is the theological question she will work through in private and never raise publicly. Expect her to arrive — through prayer, through reading, through Sheikh Abdullah, through her own slow patient reasoning — at a settled position of acceptance, and expect her then to defend that position against anyone who challenges it, including extended family in Pakistan.

**Within 5–15 years (lower confidence, higher consequence):**

Yusuf will probably predecease her. The actuarial pressure of his cardiac history, combined with the canonical pattern of South Asian male cardiovascular mortality and the narrative weight already assigned to his condition, makes this the most likely major life event of her seventh decade. Her widowhood will be the deepest test of the containment thesis. The Stage-One assessment held that her resilience under loss was role-scaffolded rather than purely characterological; widowhood removes the *wife* scaffold that has carried half her adult identity. This is the largest open question in the file (see §6.4).

She will probably not remarry. Not on doctrinal grounds — remarriage is permitted and even encouraged in her tradition — but on dispositional grounds. She is not a woman who reassembles. She is a woman who continues.

She will become, in the masjid community, an Auntie of the kind she once invoked as a disciplinary specter — *what will Auntie Ruby say?* She will be aware of this irony. She will, on her better days, leverage it: she will be the auntie who *does not* gossip, who *does not* compare daughters, who quietly intervenes when she sees a younger mother making the surveillance-for-closeness substitution she made herself.

---

## 6.3 FORK POINTS

These are the specific decision-events at which the trajectory bifurcates meaningfully. Each is named, and each has a *growth fork* and a *catastrophe fork* with the conditions that would push her one way or the other.

**Fork One: The First Time Kamala Is Hurt Badly in the Field, Post-Resurrection.**

This is coming. Kamala is operationally an X-Man now; the injury rate is non-trivial; she has already died once. The first call in the night — Logan or Storm or whoever is on the comms — will arrive within the projection window.

*Growth fork:* Muneeba absorbs the call, drives to wherever Kamala is being treated, sits in the waiting room with the same controlled stillness she has used her whole life, and on the drive home tells Yusuf, *out loud and without softening*, what she is feeling. The relational repair with Yusuf — the admission that she has been carrying this alone — opens a new register of partnered grief that will sustain her through later losses.

*Catastrophe fork:* she absorbs the call, drives to the hospital, sits in the waiting room, comes home, and tells no one anything. She begins to manage Kamala's danger the way she has been managing Yusuf's heart — by privatized hypervigilance. The container thickens. The interior pressure rises. She becomes the kind of mother whose love is felt by her child only as weight.

*Push factor toward growth:* Yusuf's continued presence and his explicit, repeated invitation to share the burden. *Push factor toward catastrophe:* Yusuf's death or decline before this event, leaving her with no co-bearer.

**Fork Two: The Mutant-Acceptance Crisis Inside Her Community.**

When (not if) a member of the Khan extended family or masjid community says something openly anti-mutant in her hearing — at a wedding, at an iftar, in the WhatsApp family group — Muneeba will have to decide, in real time, what kind of woman she is going to be in the second half of her life.

*Growth fork:* she corrects them. Publicly, calmly, with the unappealable moral authority she has spent forty years accumulating. The correction becomes a small local turning point in how Jersey City's Muslim community discusses the mutant question. She will not enjoy this role and will not seek to repeat it, but having done it once she will not be able to un-be the woman who did.

*Catastrophe fork:* she lets it pass to preserve the gathering. She tells herself she will address it privately later. She does not. The accumulated unspoken corrections become a low-grade self-betrayal that erodes the moral-certainty foundation her entire psychology rests on. This is the specific mechanism by which a woman of her profile would, in late middle age, develop the depressive presentation that the Stage-One workup ruled out at baseline.

*Push factor toward growth:* the speaker being someone with low relational cost (a distant cousin rather than her sister). *Push factor toward catastrophe:* the speaker being Yusuf's brother, or a senior aunt whose disapproval would ripple across the Karachi side of the family.

**Fork Three: The Grandchild Manifests Powers.**

If Aamir and Tyesha's child manifests mutant abilities — and given Kamala's posthumous reclassification, the genetic argument is on the table — Muneeba will face the exact problem she faced with Kamala, this time with the benefit of a completed prior iteration.

*Growth fork:* she becomes the family's experienced hand. She tells Aamir and Tyesha what she got wrong the first time. She does not pretend she got it right. The grandchild grows up in a household where the secret is not a secret, and Muneeba has been the agent of that difference. This is the most redemptive available outcome in her file.

*Catastrophe fork:* she defaults to protecting Aamir from her own prior mistakes by *withholding* what she learned, out of shame. The grandchild repeats Kamala's lonely adolescence; Aamir repeats the parental error his mother repented of in silence. Generational transmission of the very pattern she corrected for herself.

*Push factor toward growth:* having already done the verbal work of acknowledging her error to Kamala in the *Ms. Marvel* #19 register. *Push factor toward catastrophe:* never having said it out loud — and the published record is ambiguous on how fully she did.

**Fork Four: Yusuf's Death.**

*Growth fork:* the existing scaffolds — masjid, Aamir's family, Kamala (resurrected, present), Tyesha, the grandchildren — hold. She moves through the iddah, the ritual structure does what ritual structure is designed to do, and she emerges as the matriarch the family has been quietly preparing her to become. She lives another twenty years and is buried beside him.

*Catastrophe fork:* the loss arrives during a period when Kamala is off-world, or estranged, or recently killed-again; Aamir is overwhelmed by his own grief and his young family; and the masjid scaffold proves insufficient to substitute for the marital one. The containment system that survived Kamala's death — because the marriage held it — does not survive without the marriage. Symptomatic decline becomes possible: not psychotic break, but the slow somatization her file has so far refused (sleep loss, weight loss, cardiac symptoms of her own, the diagnosable depressive episode that was sub-clinical before).

*Push factor toward growth:* timing — Yusuf living long enough for the next generation to be in place. *Push factor toward catastrophe:* an early, sudden loss that arrives before she has accepted matriarch status.

**Fork Five: A Direct Threat Against the Khan Household From Kamala's Enemies.**

The probability of this is non-trivial in the published universe. If a costumed antagonist comes to the house — and someone, eventually, will — Muneeba's behavior in the acute moment is, on the evidence, predictable: she will be physically calm, she will protect whoever is closest, she will not freeze. The fork is *after*.

*Growth fork:* she accepts whatever protective arrangement Kamala and the X-Men offer, on the explicit condition that it not separate the family. She integrates the new reality without resenting the daughter who introduced it.

*Catastrophe fork:* she silently begins to resent Kamala's mission. The resentment will never be voiced; it will surface as small withdrawals — fewer visits, shorter calls, the food sent without a note. Kamala will register it and will not name it. The relationship will calcify into ritualized politeness, the precise failure mode the *Ms. Marvel* #19 revelation rescued them from once already.

---

## 6.4 OPEN QUESTIONS

The file cannot answer the following from current evidence; each is flagged for future collection.

**Does Muneeba have an interior life independent of her roles?** The published record gives almost no access to her solitary cognition. She is shown praying, cooking, working (her employment status across the runs is inconsistent — sometimes implied homemaker, sometimes implied part-time professional), managing — but rarely *thinking alone*. Whether her inner monologue, were we to access it, would reveal a rich private self or a self that has been so thoroughly given over to role that little remains in private is the single largest empirical gap in the dossier. The widowhood fork (Fork Four) will reveal the answer whether she wishes it to or not.

**What is her relationship to her own mother and to Pakistan?** The published record is conspicuously thin here. Immigration is referenced; the mother is not characterized; visits to Karachi, if any, are not depicted. This silence is itself data — it suggests either estrangement, bereavement, or a deliberate orientation away from the country of origin that she has not interrogated. Any future material that opens this door will sharply revise the etiology section of the Stage-One workup.

**What did she do, professionally or vocationally, before her children?** The file does not say. A woman of her observed competence almost certainly did *something* — taught, nursed, kept books, ran a small business with her family in Karachi. The absence of this from her own self-presentation to her children is informative: she has organized her identity around motherhood to the exclusion of prior selves. Whether this is loss, choice, or modesty is unresolved.

**How does she pray when no one can hear her?** The performative prayer register is documented; the private one is not. The difference between the two — if any — would be the most direct available index of her interiority.

**Where does her humor come from?** The dry register noted in the Stage-One workup is genuine and recurring but unexplained by the rest of the profile. Humor of that specific quality — under-stated, late-arriving, mostly unnoticed — is usually a survival of something earlier in a life. We have no access to that earlier source.

---

## 6.5 GROWTH CONDITIONS vs CATASTROPHE CONDITIONS — SYNTHESIS

**What pushes Muneeba toward growth, across all forks:**

1. *Yusuf alive and engaged.* He is, structurally, her primary growth condition. Every fork's growth path is materially easier with him present.
2. *Continued evidence-based updating.* The pattern documented in the Stage-One workup — she revises on evidence — is her single most reliable growth mechanism. Anything that gives her concrete new data (a grandchild's powers, a young mother at the masjid asking her advice, Kamala explicitly saying *thank you for changing your mind about me*) reactivates it.
3. *Explicit verbalization of what she has previously only enacted.* Her largest growth edge is the gap between what she does and what she says she has done. Forks that require her to *say it out loud* — to Aamir, to a grandchild, to herself in prayer — are the forks at which her growth becomes durable rather than situational.
4. *Role transitions that promote rather than depose her.* Matriarch, grandmother, halaqa elder: each is a structural promotion that her psychology metabolizes well.

**What pushes Muneeba toward catastrophe:**

1. *Early loss of Yusuf, before next-generation scaffolding is in place.* The single most consequential negative condition.
2. *Isolation from the masjid community.* If the Khans move (a real possibility — Jersey City property dynamics, Yusuf's care needs), the loss of the community substrate would hollow the post-Kamala compensatory structure.
3. *Repeated demands that she absorb without expression.* Her containment style works because the container is regularly emptied through ritual, partnership, and the rhythm of household labor. If the input rate exceeds the drainage rate — multiple simultaneous family crises, a Kamala death-and-resurrection cycle that begins to repeat, a global event that disrupts the masjid — the container will not break dramatically but will begin to leak somatically.
4. *Any event that forces her to choose between her daughter and her community.* The mutant-acceptance fork is the visible version of this. A larger version — a public anti-mutant action by a figure she respects, requiring her to choose sides — would be the worst-case structural pressure her psychology could face. Her growth path requires that she choose Kamala; her catastrophe path is what happens if she equivocates and then has to live with the equivocation.

---

## 6.6 TERMINAL ASSESSMENT

The likeliest single forward path, weighting the forks by their independent probabilities and her demonstrated patterns:

> Muneeba Khan will spend the next decade as the operational center of a family more complicated than the one she raised. She will manage Yusuf's decline with the competence she has always shown and will be more lonely inside that management than she will admit. She will become a grandmother and will be visibly happier in that role than her children have ever seen her. She will reach a settled, defended position on Kamala's mutancy that surprises the extended family. She will probably bury her husband. She will probably not collapse. She will probably outlive the period in which she is the family's containment system, and will probably accept — with the same quiet, slightly dry, slightly self-correcting grace that the published record has shown her capable of — being contained, in her turn, by the children she raised.

The file's working hypothesis is that **she will end better than she began**, which is not a sentence the file is often able to write. The mechanism is the one mechanism her record has reliably documented across every era of her published life: when evidence arrives, she updates; when catastrophe arrives, she holds; and when the role she has been given is finished, she accepts the next one.

The thing to watch for — the single behavioral signal that would invert this entire projection — is *withdrawal of food*. Muneeba's nurturance is canonically routed through provisioning. A Muneeba who stops cooking is a Muneeba whose containment system has begun to fail. Any future material in which she sets down a serving spoon and does not pick it back up is the file's early-warning indicator, and should be flagged for immediate Stage-Three review.

*End Stage-Two trajectory assessment. Continuous monitoring recommended; next scheduled revision upon publication of new canonical material or upon any of the named fork events.*

## Relationship Graph
### [[Kamala Khan (Ms. Marvel)]]
- Anxious-preoccupied primary attachment; the single reliable lever in her life
- Surveillance-as-love generates the secrecy it was meant to prevent — the central tragic mechanism of the early Wilson run
- Post-reveal: read into the Ms. Marvel secret; the relationship reorganizes from adversarial-protective to allied-protective
- FAILURE MODE: a hostile actor who can credibly threaten Kamala owns Muneeba's decision-making in the moment; she will lie, conceal, and act against her own theology to protect her daughter, and can be trapped inside those protective lies. If Kamala were to die in a manner Muneeba blamed herself for (a strict-mother choice that delayed disclosure), the guilt could metastasize into the depression the record otherwise rules out.
- LEVERAGE: any credible threat to Kamala; any framing that implies Muneeba's love-register cost her closeness; any forced excavation of the Aisha material in Kamala's presence

### [[Yusuf Khan]]
- Marriage as equal partnership in traditional dress; private board of two
- Decisions pressure-tested between them off-stage before executed on-stage
- FAILURE MODE: if Yusuf were lost, Muneeba would lose her primary co-regulator and her risk-modeling check; the strict register would likely intensify without his softening counterweight
- LEVERAGE: Yusuf is the channel through which she can most reliably be reached without triggering defensive escalation

### [[Aamir Khan]]
- Eldest son, devout; lower-anxiety attachment object than Kamala
- Pride in his religious seriousness; accommodation of his unconventional choices once read
- FAILURE MODE: threats to Aamir register more as a community/family-cohesion wound than as the individuated terror Kamala triggers — but compound grief (loss of both children) would breach her functional-grief ceiling
- LEVERAGE: Aamir's standing in the community; the Khan family's collective reputation

### Tyesha Hillman Khan
- Initial respectability-anxiety over community optics; full acceptance once granted interior view
- Now a daughter, not a daughter-in-law, in functional terms
- FAILURE MODE: if community pressure against the marriage intensified beyond a threshold Yusuf could not buffer, Muneeba would side with Tyesha and break with the community — a low-probability but high-cost realignment
- LEVERAGE: proves Muneeba is parochial but not bigoted; her gatekeeping is class-and-respectability based and revisable

### Sheikh Abdullah
- Delegated moral authority on lower-stakes matters; respected community elder
- Muneeba complies in public, exercises private non-compliance when his guidance conflicts with her family's good
- FAILURE MODE: a hostile actor who co-opts or impersonates the Sheikh's channel could move her on matters she would otherwise resist
- LEVERAGE: the only external moral channel she routinely defers to

### [[Bruno Carrelli]]
- Early hostility (the Italian-American non-Muslim boy too close to her daughter)
- Revised across the Wilson run into acceptance as part of Kamala's chosen family
- FAILURE MODE: any sign Bruno's presence has compromised Kamala's safety re-activates the original suspicion
- LEVERAGE: a worked example of her revision mechanism in action

### Aisha Great Grandmother
- The silence she inherited and chose to maintain
- The Inhuman/Djinn-descended matriarch whose Partition-era flight is the unspoken architecture of the family
- FAILURE MODE: forced excavation in front of her children before she has chosen the moment destabilizes the architecture she has spent a life containing
- LEVERAGE: anyone with documentary or testimonial access to Aisha's story controls Muneeba's most defended interior

### Islamic Center Of Jersey City
- Surrogate extended family; logistics, intelligence, and emotional infrastructure
- FAILURE MODE: community judgment of her parenting is a real social wound; a sustained whisper campaign would corrode her standing and her self-concept
- LEVERAGE: the social surface through which she is most easily destabilized without direct confrontation
